# 1269

A wid iumnen! Aîas n lqweôôaê d ixelwiyen, s tidep, teppen d aêerfi ayla n medden. U îeôôifen seg ubrid n Öebbi. Wid ixeznen ddheb d lfeîîa, ur ten pseddiqen deg ubrid n Öebbi, becceô iten s uâaqeb aqeôêan.

# 1270

Ass ideg ara ô$en di tmes n Loahennama, ad kwin, yissen, inyiren nnsen, ibeôdiyen nnsen, iârar nnsen. "D ayagi ay txezznem i iman nnwen. Jeôôbet ayen txezznem!"

# 1271

Ih, ar Öebbi, amvan n wagguren: mrawsin; di Tezmamt n Öebbi, ass ideg Ixleq tamurt akked igenwan. Garasen, kué ôqan. D wagi ay d ddin n ddwam. Ur ddenniset iman nnwen degsen. Nna$et ijehliyen $ef ccfa, akken i kwen nnu$en $ef ccfa. Cfut, Öebbi Iteddu d wid ipêezziben.

# 1272

Aswexxeô n waggur d timerniwt kan n tijehli. Nnetlafen yis wid ijehlen. Aseggwas a t êellen, aseggwas a t gedlen, iwakken ad wafqen amvan n wayen Igdel Öebbi. Ad êellen ayen Igdel Öebbi. Âaoben ten yir igiten nnsen. Öebbi ur Inehhu agdud ijehliyen.

# 1273

A wid iumnen! Acu kwen iu$en? Ma nnan awen: "hejjmet ar ubrid n Öebbi", a ppebrum i iman nnwen. Day kwen taâoeb tmeddurt n ddunit, sennig tin n laxeôt? Zzhu n tmeddurt n ddunit d amejîiîuê kan, zdat win n laxeôt.

# 1274

Ma ur tehjjimem ara, a kwen Iâaqeb s lqeôê, a d Iawi agdud nniven, deg umekkan nnwen. Ur T teîîuôum s wacemma. Öebbi Izmer i yal cci.

# 1275

Ma ur t tsellkem, ihi, Isellek it Öebbi, mi t ssuff$en wid ijehlen. Wissin n sin, mi llan deg ifri, mi inna i umeddakwel is: "kkes a$wbel, Öebbi, s tidep, yidne$". Issers ed Öebbi talwit iS fellas, Iâawen it s iâsekriwen, ur ten twalam. Isse$li mavi awal n wid ijehlen. Awal n Öebbi, neppa, aâlay sennig akw. Öebbi d Uzmir, d Bab n ûûwab.

# 1276

Hejjmet fessusit u ééayit, juhdet s wayla nnwen akked yiman nnwen, deg ubrid n Öebbi. Ppif wakka i kunwi, lemmer teéôim.

# 1277

Lemmer d aba$uô isehlen, d inig wezzilen, yili vefôen k in. Maca, $wezzif fellasen umecwaô. Ad ggalen s Öebbi: "lemmer nezmir, yili neffe$ yidwen". Nn$an iman nnsen, Öebbi Iéôa ar nitni, war ccekk, d ikeddaben.

# 1278

Ad ak Isemmeê Öebbi! Acimi i sen tserêev? Ard ak d iban anwi innan tidep, a ppissinev ikeddaben.

# 1279

Ur ak d ssutren ara tsriê, wid iumnen s Öebbi akked wass aneggaru, mi juhden s wayla nnsen akked yiman nnsen. Öebbi Issen wid ipêezziben.

# 1280

I k issutren tsriê, d wid ur numin s Öebbi akked wass aneggaru. Cukken wulawen nnsen, d$a, s ucukku nnsen, kukran.

# 1281

Lemmer b$in tuff$a, yili heggan as d ayen ilaqen. Maca, Iugi Öebbi ad ppucegâan, Iurez iten. Nnan asen: "qqimet d wid iqqimen".

# 1282

Lemmer ffi$en yidwen, ar awen rnun siwa ccwal. War ccekk, ad kecmen garawen, b$an ahewwel nnwen. Kra segwen ssemêasen asen. Öebbi Issen imednas.

# 1283

Ni$ b$an, si zik, ahewwel. Sxeôben ak lumuô, armi d tusa tidep. Ivehô ed lameô n Öebbi, nitni ur b$in.

# 1284

Garasen win id innan: "serreê iyi, ur iyi gar di lfetna"! Day ur $lin ara di lfetna? Loahennama, s tidep, a ppezzi i ijehliyen.

# 1285

Ma iusa k id yise$ ad $weblen. Ma tusa k id twa$it, ad inin: "ni$, iu$ lêal, neqva lameô nne$". Ad wexxôen, zzhan.

# 1286

Ini: "ur a$ ipêaz wacemma, siwa ayen i $ Iura Öebbi". Neppa d Bab nne$. £ef Öebbi ara ppeklen lmumnin.

# 1287

Ini: "acu teggunim ad ivôu yidne$, siwa yiwen si sin ise$iyen? Nekwni negguni a kwen Iwwet Öebbi, s uâaqeb ara d iasen s$uôeS, ne$ seg ifassen nne$. Ihi gganit, nekwni a neggani yidwen".

# 1288

Ini: "seddqet, teb$am ne$ tugim, d ayen ur neppwaqbal segwen, d awez$i. Kunwi, s tidep, d agdud iballa$en".

# 1289

Ay sen ikksen a tepwaqbal ssadaqa nnsen, imi kan jehlen, s tidep, ar Öebbi akked Umazan iS, u s laâgez kan ay d ppasen ar tpéallit, s usmiglez kan ay pseddiqen.

# 1290

Ur k ippaâoab wayla nnsen, ne$ tarwa nnsen. Ib$a kan Öebbi a ten Iâaqeb yissen di tmeddurt n ddunit, ad iffe$ ôôuê nnsen, nitni d ijehliyen.

# 1291

Ad ggalen s Öebbi, ar nitni, war ccekk, segwen. Ur nitni segwen, maca d agdud iugaden.

# 1292

Lemmer ad afen ssôan, ne$ ifran, ne$ anda ara kecmen, ad ôuêen $uôes s tazla.

# 1293

Garasen, wid ikkaten deg k, $ef ssadaqat. Ma ippunefk asen segsent, ad ôavin, ma ur asen ippunefk, ad neêwen.

# 1294

Lemmer nitni, s tidep, ôuvan ayen i sen Ifka Öebbi akked Umazan iS, u nnan d: "nesteqnaâ s Öebbi. Ad a$ d Ifk, si lfevl iS, Öebbi akked Umazan iS. Ih, d Öebbi i$ef neô$eb".

# 1295

Ssadaqat siwa i ime$ban, iéawaliyen, i wid ice$wlen degsent, i usemlili n wulawen, i userreê imeêbas, i imeîîulba, i ubrid n Öebbi, i win d ifka ubrid. D aêeppem s$uô Öebbi. Öebbi d Amusnaw, d Bab n ûûwab.

# 1296

Garasen, wid icettmen deg Umazan, qqaôen: "neppa d aêessas". Ini: "d aêessas n lxiô i kunwi. Iumen s Öebbi, iumen lmumnin. D aêunu i wid iumnen segwen". I wid icettmen deg Umazan n Öebbi, aâaqeb aqeôêan.

# 1297

Ad awen ggalen s Öebbi, iwakken a kwen ôavin. Öebbi akked Umazan iS, Iklal kteô a T ôavin, lemmer llin d lmumnin.

# 1298

Day ur éôin ara ar, win ixuûmen Öebbi akked Umazan iS, i neppa times n Loahennama, ad iwekkeô degs? D wagi ay d ddell abarar.

# 1299

Ixabiten ugaden ad asen d ters tsuôep, ad asen tessken i illan deg ulawen nnsen. Ini: "mmaâlket. Öebbi, s tidep, a d Issuffe$ ayen tugadem".

# 1300

Ma testeqsav ten, a d inin, war ccekk: "la nheddeô kan, nepqessiô". Ini: "day la tettihim di Öebbi akked issekniyen iS, akked Umazan iS?

# 1301

Ur steôoiâat. Ni$ tu$alem ar tijehli, deffir liman nnwen". Ma Nsemmeê i urbaâ segwen, a Naâqeb arbaâ, imi nitni llan d ibe$wviyen.

# 1302

Ixabiten akked txabitin, wa ippameô i wa, ayen n dir, ppemyegdalen lewqama, pcuddun ifassen nnsen. Ppun Öebbi, Ippu ten. Ih, ixabiten d iballa$en.

# 1303

Iwaââed Öebbi, i ixabiten, txabitin, akked ijehliyen, times n Loahennama, degs ad wekkôen. Beôka ten. Ixza ten Öebbi. Fellasen aâaqeb imezgi,

# 1304

am imezwura nnwen. Llan ifen kwen tazmert, $elben kwen ayla, tarwa. Zhan deg umur nnsen, tezham deg umur nnwen, akken zhan imezwura nnwen deg umur nnsen. Teccvem akken ccven nitni. Widak, mêan igiten nnsen di ddunit, di laxeôt. Widak d imexsuôen.

# 1305

Day ur ten id iusa ara usali imezwura nnsen? Agdud n Nuê, Âad, Tamud, agdud n Ibôahim, At Median, tid ippin. Usan ten id imazanen nnsen, s ubeggen. Ur ten Idennis Öebbi, maca llan dennisen iman nnsen.

# 1306

Lmumnin, argaz tameîîut, d imeddukal wa n wa. Ppamôen lewqama, pgeddilen ayen n dir. Péallan, pzekkin, ppa$en awal i Öebbi akked Umazan iS. Wigi, ad Iêun Öebbi fellasen. Ih, Öebbi d Uzmir, d Bab n ûûwab.

# 1307

Iwaââed Öebbi i lmumnin, argaz tameîîut, leonanat, ddawat sen isaffen ppazzalen, ad wekkôen degsen; ixxamen igerzen di leonanat n Âaden, akked llza s$uô Öebbi - iten i$elben akw -. D wagi ay d rrbeê ameqwôaêan.

# 1308

A Nnbi! Jahed ijehliyen akked ixabiten. Iqsiê $uôsen. Axxam nnsen d Loahennama, d taggara tucmip!

# 1309

Ggulen s Öebbi ur d nnin, wanag nnan awal n tijehli. Jehlen deffir wannuz nnsen. Vemâen ayen iwumi ur wâan. Ur êzinen imi iten I$at, si lfevl iS, Öebbi akked Umazan iS. Ma steôoâen, yif it i nitni. Ma wexxôen, a ten Iâaqeb Öebbi s leqôeê, di ddunit, di laxeôt. Ur sâun, di tmurt, bab ne$ amâiwen.

# 1310

# 1311

# 1312

# 1313

# 1314

Wid ipqeôôiven di lmumnin i ib$an ad seddqen, u deg wid i iufan siwa tazmert nnsen, d$a ttihin fellasen; ad Ittihi Öebbi fellasen. Fellasen aâaqeb aqeôêan.

# 1315

# 1316

# 1317

# 1318

# 1319

# 1320

Ur k ippaâoab wayla nnsen, ne$ dderya nnsen. Öebbi Ib$a kan a ten Iâaqeb yissen di ddunit, ad asen teffe$ taôwiêt nitni d ijehliyen.

# 1321

Ma ters ed tsuôep: "amnet s Öebbi, jahdet akked Umazan iS", imeôkantiyen nnsen a k ssutren tsriê, ad inin: "anef ane$ ar wid iqqimen".

# 1322

Öuvan ad ilin akked wid igwran. Ppusel$en wulawen nnsen, ur fehhmen.

# 1323

Maca, amazan akked wid iumnen yides, jehden s wayla nnsen akked yiman nnsen. Widak, nnsen lxiô. Widak, d nitni ara irebêen.

# 1324

# 1325

# 1326

Ur telli tuzzma $ef uôhifen, imuvan, wid ur nufi ara fken, ma neûêen ar Öebbi akked Umazan iS. Ur telli tuzzma $ef iâaôviyen. Öebbi Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu.

# 1327

Am akken, i wid ik id iusan a ten tneqqlev, tenniv: "ur awen ufi$ ara kwen ineqqlen". U$alen, allen feggvent seg imeîîawen, $weblen imi ur ufin ara sedqen.

# 1328

# 1329

# 1330

Ad awen gren Öebbi, mi d tu$alem $uôsen, iwakken ad asen tanfem. Wexxeôt asen; nitni, s tidep, d laâôuô; axxam nnsen d Loahennama, d aqeîîi n wayen keppben.

# 1331

# 1332

# 1333

Ger waâôaben n ucluê, wid iêesben ayen seddqen d tabzert. Ggunin a ppekêes fellawen teswiât. Fellasen abeddel adiran n teswiât! Öebbi Issel, Issen.

# 1334

# 1335

Imenza i izwaren, seg iminigen, imâiwnen, akked wid i ten iâanden ar lewqama, Iôuva ten Öebbi, ôuvan T. Ihegga yasen d leonanat, ddawat sen isaffen ppazzalen, ad wekkôen degsen, i lebda. D wagi ay d rrbeê ameqwôaêan.

# 1336

# 1337

# 1338

# 1339

# 1340

# 1341

Wiyav pganin lameô n Öebbi, a ten Iâaqeb, ne$ ad asen Issuref. Öebbi d Amusnaw, d Bab n ûûwab.

# 1342

Wid irran loamaâ i lemveôôa akked tijehli, i lefôaq ger lmumnin; d taxettalt i wid, iu$ lêal, llan pna$en Öebbi akked Umazan iS, ad ggalen, war ccekk: "ay neb$a siwa lewqama". Ad Icehhed Öebbi ar nitni, s tidep, d ikeddaben.

# 1343

Ur ppili, degs, d awez$i. Iklal kteô, tilin ik, loamaâ ibnan $ef uêezzeb, seg wass amenzu. Degs irgazen i iêemmlen ad izdigen. Öebbi Iêemmel izedganen.

# 1344

# 1345

# 1346

# 1347

Wid isteôoâen, wid iâabden, wid ipcekkiôen, ixelwiyen, wid iîîinizen, wid ikennun, wid ippamôen lewqama, wid ipgeddilen ayen n dir, wid ipêaraben $ef tlisa n Öebbi ... Becceô lmumnin.

# 1348

Ur issefk ara i Nnbi akked wid iumnen, ad ssutren ad pwasemmêen imcurak, xas ppilin asen, ma iban asen d ar, nitni, war ccekk, d at tmes.

# 1349

# 1350

Ur p Ixeddem Öebbi, ad Itlef agdud mbaâd ma Inha ten, alamma i sen Ibeggen acu ara êezzben. Öebbi, s tidep, Issen yal cci.

# 1351

# 1352

Ni$ Issuref Öebbi i Nnbi akked iminigen, akked imâiwnen i iddan yides, di lweqt uwâiô, mbaâd ma qôib nneqlaben wulawen n urbaâ segsen. Sinna, Issuref asen. Ih, Neppa, i nitni, dUmâin, d'Aênin.

# 1353

U i krav id igwran, armi, tamurt iwsâan, tediyyeq fellasen. Vaqen deg iman nnsen. Ufan ur illi ssôan si Öebbi, siwa Neppa. Sinna, Issuref asen, akken ad steôoâen. Öebbi, s tidep, Issuruf, Ipêunu.

# 1354

A wid iumnen! Ëezzbet i Öebbi, ilit seg imawlan n tidep.

# 1355

Ur issefk ara i imezda$ n Lmadina, d wayen i sen d izzin n waâôaben n ucluê, ad gwrin deffir Umazan n Öebbi, ne$ ad smenyafen iman nnsen i iman is. # 1356

# 1357

# 1358

A wid iumnen! Nna$et ijehliyen i kwen iqeôben. Ad afen, $uôwen, teqseê. Cfut, Öebbi Ippili d wid ipêezziben.

# 1359

# 1360

Ma d wid iwumi blan wulawen, terna ammus i wammus nnsen. Mmuten u nitni d ijehliyen.

# 1361

Day ur walan ara, ar nitni la d sskaren lfetna, yal aseggwas, yiwen ubrid ne$ berdayen? Sinna, ur steôoiâen, ur d smektayen.

# 1362

# 1363

Ni$ iusa kwen id Umazan seg iman nnwen. èéay fellas laâtab nnwen. Ipêarab fellawen, d umâin, d aênin i lmumnin.

# 1364

# 1365

# 1366

# 1367

Ih, Mass nnwen d Öebbi, i Ixelqen tamurt akked igenwan di sdis wussan. Sinna, Iâannec $ef usgeld, Iseyyi lameô. Ur illi umcafaâ siwa ma Iâammed as. D wagi ay d Öebbi, Mass nnwen. Ihi, âabdet eP. Day ur d tesmektayem ara?

# 1368

£uôeS akw tu$alin nnwen. Lemâahda n Öebbi d tidep. Ih, Inezzu axlaq, Ippales, iwakken ad Ikafi wid iumnen u xeddmen ayen ilhan, s lmizan. I wid ijehlen, tissit iô$an, aâaqeb aqeôêan, imi llan jehlen.

# 1369

D Neppa i Irran iîij d lefnaô, aggur d tafat. Iwezn as tiswaâin, iwakken a ppissinem amvan iseggwasen, akked leêsab. Ur Ixliq Öebbi ayagi, siwa s tidep. Ipfeûûil issekniyen i ugdud issnen.

# 1370

S tidep, di lemgarda ger yiv akked wass, akked wayen Ixleq Öebbi di tmurt akked igenwan, ard issekniyen i ugdud i ipêezziben.

# 1371

Ih, wid ur negguni ara timlilit yidne£, i tqennaâ tmeddurt di ddunit, u rekden degs, d wid i istehzan $ef issekniyen nne£.

# 1372

# 1373

Ih, wid iumnen u xeddmen ayen ilhan, a ten Inhu Mass nnsen, s liman nnsen. Ad ppazzalen isaffen seddawat sen, di leonanat isaâdiyen.

# 1374

Anuju nnsen degs: "gedha s yissek a Öebbi"! Azul nnsen d: "tifrat". Anuju nnsen aneggaru: "ccekôan i Öebbi, Mass imavalen".

# 1375

Lemmer ad Iaâoel Öebbi cceôô ar imdanen, akken nitni êaren $ef lxiô, yili ibbwev asen lajel nnsen. A Nanef i wid ur negguni ara timlilit yidne£, ad ddebdben di lbe$wv nnsen.

# 1376

Amdan, ma iêuza t ccqa, ad a£ £ d isiwel, iééel, iqqim ne$ ibedd. Mi s Nekkes ccqa s, ad iteddu amzun ur d inuj $uône£ilmend n ccqa i t iêuzan. Akka ay ppucebêen igiten nnsen i imaâfan.

# 1377

Ni$ Nesqucc isuta, uqbel nnwen, imi densen. Ussan d $uôsen imazanen nnsen, s ubeggen, ur llin d wid ara iamnen. Akka ay Nepqeîîi agdud ibe$wviyen.

# 1378

Sinna, Nerra kwen d igensas di tmurt, deffir sen, a Nwali amek ara txedmem.

# 1379

Ma $ôan asen issekniyen nne£ iberrzen, wid ur negguni ara timlilit yidne£, ad inin: "awi d Leqwôan nniven, ne$ beddel it". Ini: "ur felli a t beddle$, s leb$i n yiman iw. Teddu$ kan akked wayen iyi d ippuweêêan. Nek ugade$, ma xedâa$ Mass iw, aâaqeb n wass ameqwôaêan".

# 1380

Ini: "lemmer i S ihwi i Öebbi, ur awen t id mli$, ur awen t id mmekti$. Ni$ zed$e$ yidwen tameddurt, uqbel is. Day ur tfehmem ara"?

# 1381

Anwa i idensen kteô, ger win id igren tikerkas $ef Öebbi, ne$ win inekôen issekniyen iS? Ih, ur rebêen ibe$wviyen.

# 1382

La âabden, war Öebbi, ayen ur ten neîîuôu, ur ten nenfaâ. La qqaôen: "wigi d imcafâen nne$ ar Öebbi". Ini: "day a pxebbôem Öebbi $ef wayen ur Issin, di tmurt akked igenwan"? Gedha s yiS! I Aâlay sennig wayen pcaraken!

# 1383

Llan imdanen d yiwen n lois kan. Sinna, mgaraden. Lemmer ur d izwar ara wawal, s$uô Mass ik, ad yili uêuddu, garasen, $ef wayen i$ef mgaraden.

# 1384

La qqaôen: "a lemmer id irs $uôes ussekni n Mass is"! Ini: "tabavnit ar Öebbi kan. Ihi, gganit. Nek, yidwen, seg wid iggunin".

# 1385

Ma Nesêess i imdanen aêunu, deffir twa$it i ten iêuzan, atnan la ppandin i issekniyen nne£. Ini: "Öebbi Yif akw akken Ip$awal di tiêeôci". Imersulen nne£, s tidep, pparun ayen teppandim.

# 1386

Neppa i kwen Ippawin di lberr, di yill. Alamma, mi tellam di lembwabeô, teppedum degsen s wavu uûwib, feôêen yis, tusa d tbucivant $uôsen, ppasent ed lemwao $uôsen, si yal tama, êulfan a d tezzi fellasen. Naâôen Öebbi, s lqaâida i Neppa: "ma Tsellkev a$ si tagi, ar a nili seg wid isnemmiren".

# 1387

Mi ten Isellek, imiren u$alen be$wven di tmurt, war ssebba. A yimdanen! Lbe$wv nnwen, siwa $ef yiman nnwen. Zzhu di tmeddurt n ddunit, sinna, $uône£ tu$alin nnwen, ad awen Nmel ayen txeddmem.

# 1388

Amedya n tmeddurt di ddunit, am aman kan. Nesse$li ten id seg igenni, xelven akked im$an n tmurt, iseg teppen imdanen akked lmal. Mi tcebbeê tmurt, tu$al d tuzyint, $ilen, imezda$ is, ar deg ufus nnsen ay tella. Iusa p id lameô nne£, deg iv, ne$ deg wass, Nerra p d ahicuô, amzun ur teoouoeg ass izeryen. Akka ay Nfeûûel issekniyen i ugdud ipxemmimen.

# 1389

Inecced Öebbi s axxam n tifrat. Inehhu win i S ihwan, ar ubrid uwqim.

# 1390

I wid iweqmen, lewqama, ternuv as. Udmawen nnsen, ur ten ipnal bufsus, ne$ ddell. Widak, d at Loennet, nitni, degs ad wekkôen.

# 1391

Aqeîîi n wid id ibbwin tucmitin, d tucmip itent icban. Ad ndellen. Ur sâun amenêul ar Öebbi. Amzun $ummen wudmawen nnsen, s ccevyat n yiv iberkanen. Widak d at tmes, nitni, degs, ad wekkôen.

# 1392

Ass ideg ara ten Nfesser akw, a Nini, imiren, i wid icurken: "imukan nnwen, kunwi akked icriken nnwen"! Sinna Nessemfaôaq iten. A d inin, icriken nnsen: "maççi d nekwni ay tâabdem.

# 1393

Ad Iqadd Öebbi, d Anagi garane$ yidwen, ar ur d necliâ deg uâbbed nnwen".

# 1394

Din, yal amdan ad iwali ayen iwasa. Ad u$alen ar Öebbi, Bab nnsen n tidep. Itelf iten wayen d snulfuyen.

# 1395

Ini: "anwa ikwen Ip$itin seg igenni akked tmurt? Anwa ay d Bab n tmejjin akked yiéôi? Anwa id Issuffu$en amuddir si lmegget, id Issuffu$en lmegget seg umuddir? Anwa i Iseyyin lameô"? A d inin: "d Öebbi". Ini: "ihi, day ur tepêezzibem ara"?

# 1396

D wagi ay d Öebbi, Mass nnwen n tidep. Deffir tidep, acu i illan, siwa ttelfan? Ihi, acimi texdâam?

# 1397

Akka i iûaô wawal n Mass ik, $ef wid ixedmen tucmitin. Ih, nitni ur ppamnen.

# 1398

Ini: "day illa ger icriken nnwen, win id inzan lxelq, sinna, iules as d"? Ini: "Öebbi inezzu lxelq, sinna, Ippales as d. Ihi, amek ara twexxôem"?

# 1399

Ini: "day illa, ger icriken nnwen, win i inehhun ar tidep"? Ini: "Öebbi Inehhu ar tidep. Win Inehhun ar tidep, day ur Yif ara, akken Iklal tikli yideS, win ur nennehhu, siwa ma ipwanha? Acu ikwen iu$en? Amek tepseyyim"?

# 1400

Tegwti, segsen, teddun kan d nnwaya. Nnwaya, war ccekk, ur tebbwi acemma si tidep. Ih, Öebbi Issen acu xeddmen.

# 1401

Leqwôan agi ur d innulfa ara, war Öebbi. Maca, d atebbet n wayen it id izwaren, d afeûûel n Tezmamt, ur degs ccekk, s$uô Mass imavalen.

# 1402

Ne$ la qqaôen: "isnulfa t id". Ini: "awit ed tasuôep i t icban, neccdet seg wanda tzemrem, war Öebbi, ma tessawalem tidep".

# 1403

Xaîi, skaddben ayen ur nekcim di tmusni nnsen, ur ten id iusi usefhem is. Akka ay skaddben, wid i ten id izwaren. Wali, ihi, amek tevôa d imednas.

# 1404

Garasen, wid iumnen yis; garasen, wid ur numin yis. Mass ik Yif akw akken Issen ifessaden.

# 1405

Ma skaddben k, ini: "i nek igiten iw, i kunwi igiten nnwen. Ur teppkam deg wayen xedme$, ur ppka$ deg wayen txedmem".

# 1406

# 1407

Garasen, llan wid i k ipmuqulen. Day tzemrev a ppenhuv ider$alen, ma llan ur pwalin?

# 1408

Öebbi, s tidep, ur Iddennis imdanen, s wacemma, maca imdanen densen iman nnsen.

# 1409

Ass ideg ara ten Ifser, amzun sâaddan kan saâa n wass, ad msaâqalen. Ni$ xesôen wid iskaddben timlilit d Öebbi. Ur pwanhan.

# 1410

Ad ak Nessken kra seg wayen i sen Nâahed, ne$ a k id Nawi $uône£. Ihi, $uône£ tu$alin nnsen. Sinna, Öebbi d Anagi n wayen xeddmen.

# 1411

I yal lois, amazan. Ma iusa d umazan nnsen, a ppefru garasen s lmizan, ur pwadensen.

# 1412

Qqaôen: "melmi lemâahda agi, ma tessawalem tidep?

# 1413

Ini: "ur mlike$ i iman iw vveôô, ne$ aba$uô, siwa ayen Ib$a Öebbi. Yal lois s lajel is". Ma iusa d lajel nnsen, ur t swexxiôen s saâa, ur t id sseqôaben.

# 1414

Ini: "acu twalam, ma iusa kwen id uâaqeb iS, deg iv, ne$ deg wass? Acimi êaren $uôeS ibe$wviyen?

# 1415

D$a, ma iusa d, a ppamnem yis? Tura, aql akwen t$eûbem fellas".

# 1416

# 1417

# 1418

Xas ad isâu, yal amdan idensen, i illan di tmurt, ur d ifeddu yis. Ffren nndama mi walan aâaqeb. Aêuddu garasen, s lmizan, ur pwadensen.

# 1419

Day, s tidep, maççi n Öebbi i illan di tmurt akked igenwan? Ih, day lemâahda n Öebbi maççi d tidep? Maca, tegwti segsen ur ssinen.

# 1420

Neppa Issidir, Ineqq. £uôeS ara tu$alem.

# 1421

A yimdanen! Ni$ iusa kwen id unabi s$uô Mass nnwen, akked ccfa n wayen iblan ulawen, akked nnhaya, akked uêunu i lmumnin.

# 1422

Ini: "s lfevl n Öebbi akked uêunu S, s waya, xas ad feôêen". Yif ayen pkemmimen.

# 1423

Ini: "twalam ayen i wen d Issers Öebbi n ôôeéq? Terram segs leêlal d leêôam". Ini: "Iâammed awen Öebbi, ne$ tesnulfam d $ef Öebbi"?

# 1424

Acu ara meyyzen, ass n tnekra, wid id igren tikerkas $ef Öebbi? Ih, Öebbi d Bab n lfevl af imdanen, maca tegwti segsen ur snemmiren.

# 1425

Ur teppiliv di liêala, ur temmalev si Leqwôan, ur tepce$wilem di kra, mebla ma Nella d Inagan nnwen, mara tweqmem. Lmizan ubelkim di tmurt u deg igenni, ur idrig i Mass ik. Akken seddaw waya, ne$ sennig es. Akw, di Tezmamt ipbegginen.

# 1426

# 1427

# 1428

a ten beccôen s lxiô di tmeddurt n ddunit, di laxeôt. Ur illi ubeddel deg wawalen n Öebbi. D wagi ay d rrbeê ameqwôaêan.

# 1429

# 1430

S tidep, day maççi n Öebbi i illan deg igenwan, i illan di tmurt? D acu îîafaôen wid ipnujun, war Öebbi, ar icriken? Ïîafaôen kan nnwaya. Oaââlen kan.

# 1431

Neppa, i wen Irran iv i ureyyeê nnwen, ass iwakken a pwalim. Deg waya, s tidep, d issekniyen i ugdud isellen.

# 1432

Nnan: "Öebbi Isâa aqcic. Gedha s yiS! Neppa d Ameôkanti. IneS i illan deg igenwan, i illan di tmurt. Ur tesâim adabu $ef waya. Day a d tinim $ef Öebbi, ayen ur tessinem"?

# 1433

Ini: "s tidep, wid id igren tikerkas $ef Öebbi, ur rebêen".

# 1434

Zzhu di ddunit, sinna, $uône£ tu$alin nnsen. D$a, ad asen Nsâaddi aâaqeb uqsiê, imi llan jehlen.

# 1435

# 1436

Ma twexxôem, ur awen ssuture$ taqdiât. Ih, taqdiât iw ar Öebbi kan. Felli lameô ad ili$ seg imvuâen.

# 1437

Skaddben t. Nsellek it, akked wid illan yides, di lbabuô. Nerra ten d igensas. Ne$meq wid iskaddben issekniyen nne£. Wali amek tevôa d wid ippunedôen.

# 1438

# 1439

# 1440

Mi ten id tusa tidep, s$uône£, nnan: "wagi, ih, d ssêur n ûûeê".

# 1441

# 1442

# 1443

# 1444

# 1445

# 1446

# 1447

# 1448

# 1449

# 1450

# 1451

# 1452

# 1454

# 1455

Tura! Ni$ zik taâûav, telliv seg ifessaden.

# 1456

Assa, a Nsellek loeppa k, a d tegwri d assekni i wid ara k id ineûfen. Aîas n medden, s tidep, stehzan deg issekniyen nne£.

# 1457

Ni$ Nessers At Isôail deg umkan umâin, u N$at iten s wayen ilhan. Ur mgaraden armi ten id tusa tussna. Ih, Mass ik ad Iêudd garasen, ass n tnekra, ilmend n wayen i$ef llan mgaraden.

# 1458

xas usan ten id akw issekniyen, alamma walan aâaqeb aqeôêan.

# 1462

# 1463

# 1464

Ur ippamen umdan siwa ma Irad Öebbi. Isdullu wid ur nfehhem ara.

# 1465

# 1466

# 1467

# 1468

# 1469

Sbedd udem ik i ddin, s umili ar tidep, ur ppili seg imcurak.

# 1470

Ur pnuju, war Öebbi, ar wayen ur k inefâan, ur k iîîuôôun. Ma txedmev akken, keçç, imiren, a ppiliv seg imednas.

# 1471

Ma Isâadda fellak Öebbi ccqa, ur ak illi ujebbaô siwa Neppa. Ma Irad ak lxiô, ur illi usebîîel i lfevl iS. Ippak it i win i S ihwan, deg ixdimen iS. Neppa Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu.

# 1472

Ini: "a yimdanen! Ni$ tusa kwen id tidep s$uô Mass nnwen! Win ipwanhan, ipwanha kan i iman is; win innetlafen, innetlef kan i iman is. Ur lli$, nek, d awkil nnwen".

# 1473

Ddu d wayen ik ed ippuweêêan, eûbeô ard Iêudd Öebbi. Neppa, Yif akw imêaddan.

# 1474

Alô. Tazmamt, issekniyen iS ppuûewwben, sinna, ppufeûûlen s$uô Uûwib i Ipwaxebbôen.

# 1475

Ur âabdet siwa Öebbi. Nek, s$uôeS $uôwen, d aneddaô u d abcir.

# 1476

Ssutret ssmaê i Mass nnwen, steôoâet aS, ad Ifeôôeo fellawen afeôôeo ilhan, ar lajel ipwassnen. Ippak lfevl iS i yal bab n lfevl. Ma twexxôem, nekk ugade$ a ppeppuâqbem, ass ameqwran.

# 1477

Tu$alin nnwen, ar Öebbi. Neppa Izmer i yal cci.

# 1478

# 1479

Ur illi lweêc di tmurt, mebla ma illa ôôeéq is ar Öebbi. Issen tanezdu$t is, tanîelt is. Meôôa, di Tezmamt ipbegginen.

# 1480

D Neppa i Ixelqen tamurt akked igenwan di sdis wussan. Asgeld iS illa $ef waman. A kwen Ijeôôeb anwi segwen ara ixedmen ayen ilhan, sennig wiyav. Ma tenniv: "ih, kunwi a d tekkrem deffir tmeppant nnwen", wid ijehlen, war ccekk, a d inin: "ayagi, kan, d ssêur n ûûeê".

# 1481

Ma Neswexxeô asen aâaqeb ar imir ipwassnen, war ccekk, a d inin: "d acu iT iîîfen"? Ass ideg ara ten id iawev, day illa wa ara ten iveôôfen segs? Ad asen izzi wayen i$ef pmmaâliken.

# 1482

Ma Nesêess i umdan aêunu nne ̈£, sinna, Nekkes as t, atan ad iayes, ad ijhel.

# 1483

# 1484

Kkes ed wid iûebbôen, ixeddmen ayen ilhan. I widak ssmaê akked tikci meqqwôen.

# 1485

Ahat teppaoav kra n wayen ik ed ippuweêêan. Pzemmiven yis idmaren ik mara qqaôen: "a lemmer i s d irs ugerruj, ne$ idda d, yides, lmelk"! Keçç d aneddaô kan. Öebbi d Awkil n yal cci.

# 1486

Ne$ ad inin: "isnulfa t id". Ini: "awit ed, s usnulfu, mraw n tsuôtin am neppa. Naâôet ayen iwumi tzemrem, war Öebbi, ma tessawalem tidep".

# 1487

Ma ur awen d rran ara, cfut ar irs ed kan s tussna n Öebbi, ar ur illi ôebbi siwa Neppa. Ihi, ma kunwi d imvuâen?

# 1488

I wid ib$an tameddurt n ddunit akked ôôêuê is, a Nkafi, degs, igiten nnsen, ur asen Ntekkes.

# 1489

Widak, ur ppafen, di laxeôt, siwa times. Ad i$li wayen ûenâen degs; inqev wayen xeddmen.

# 1490

Day win iddan d ubeggen, s$uô Mass is, u immal as t unagi s$uôeS...? U, uqbel is, Tazmamt n Musa, d nnhaya u d aêunu. Wigi umnen yis. Win i p inekôen, seg ikubar, ppaâud is d times. Ur ppili di ccekk fellas. Neppa, ih, d tidep s$uô Mass ik. Maca, tegwti n medden ur ppamnen.

# 1491

Anwa idensen sennig win id isnulfan tikerkas $ef Öebbi? Wigi a d rsen i Mass nnsen. A d inin inagan: "d wigi i iskaddben $ef Mass nnsen". Day Öebbi ur Ixezzu yara imednas?

# 1492

I isîixxiôen seg ubrid n Öebbi, i t issarmen d uâwij, nitni ur uminen s laxeôt?

# 1493

Wigi, ur sfunnugen di tmurt, ur asen illi bab, war Öebbi. Fellasen aâaqeb ar wayev. Ur zmiren ad slen, ur pwalin.

# 1494

D wigi i isxesôen iman nnsen. Itelf iten wayen d snulfuyen.

# 1495

# 1496

# 1497

Amedya n snat n trebbuyaâ am uder$al, uâééug, akked win ipwalin, win isellen. Day âadlen sin imedyaten agi? Day ur d tesmektayem ara?

# 1498

Ni$ Nuzen ed Nuê i ugdud is: "nek d aneddaô nnwen ipbegginen,

iwakken ur tâabdem siwa Öebbi. Nek ugaded aâaqeb fellawen, ass aqeôhan".

# 1500

Nnan imvebbôen, wid ijehlen, seg ugdud is: "keçç, $uône$, d amdan am nekwni. Nwala, d ôôdiyen nne$, kan, war ameyyez, i k ivefôen. Ur nwala s wacu i $ tifem. Xaîi, nêesb ikwen d ikeddaben".

# 1501

Inna: "a yagdud iw! Acu twalam ma ddi$ d ubeggen n Mass iw? Ifka yi d aêunu s$uôeS. Idreg fellawen. Day a t nêeppem fellawen, ma kunwi tugim t?

# 1502

A yagdud iw! Ur awen ssuture$ ayla, ilmend is; taqdiât iw ar Öebbi kan. Ur ppara$, nek, wid iumnen. S tidep, ad mlilen d Mass nnsen. Maca, nek wala$ kwen d agdud ur nessin.

# 1503

A yagdud iw! Acu ara yi isellken seg ufus n Öebbi, lemmer i ten rri$ akin, day ur d tesmektayem ara?

# 1504

Ur awen qqaôe$: $uôi lexzayen n Öebbi. Ur ssine$ tabavnit. Ur qqaôe$: nek d lmelk. Ur qqaôe$ i wid êeqôent wallen nnwen: ur asen Ippak ara Öebbi lxiô, d awez$i. Yif akw Öebbi akken Iéôa, i illan deg iman nnsen. Mulac ad ili$ seg imednas".

# 1505

Nnan: "a Nuê! Ni$ tnamrev a$, tessugtev a$ anamer. Ihi, awi ya$ d ayen i $ tâahdev, ma tessawalev tidep".

# 1506

Inna: "d Öebbi kan ar awen t id Iawin, ma ihwa yaS. Kunwi ur tesfunnugem.

# 1507

Xas b$i$ a kwen neûêe$, ur tesfaydayam seg wanûaê iw, ma Ib$a Öebbi a kwen Itlef. Neppa d Mass nnwen; tu$alin nnwen $uôeS".

# 1508

Ne$ qqaôen: "isnulfa t id". Ini: "ma snulfa$ t id, lbe$wv iw i yiri w. Nek, ur ppka$ di lbe$wv nnwen".

# 1509

Ippuweêêa d i Nuê: "ur ippamen yiwen, d awez$i, seg ugdud ik, siwa wid illan umnen. Ihi, ur k icqi wayen xeddmen.

# 1510

Eûnaâ lbabuô, ger wallen nne£, s uweêêi nne£. Ur iyI d pmeslay $ef wid idensen, war ccekk, ad $emqen".

# 1511

La iûennaâ lbabuô. Yal tikelt ara âaddin $uôes imvebbôen n ugdud is, tkaâriren fellas. Inna: "ma temmaâlkem degne$, ihi, a nemmaâlek degwen akken temmaâlkem.

# 1512

Deqqal a ppeéôem, u$uô ara d ias uâaqeb ara t isdullen, ara iêaz uâaqeb imezgi".

# 1513

Alamma, mi d iusa lameô nne£, la pfeggiven igwefran d ihedman, Nenna: "awi degs tayuga n yal ûûenf, tawacult ik - siwa wid i$ef id izwar wawal -, akked wid iumnen". Drus kan i iumnen yides.

# 1514

Inna: "rekbet degs, s yisem n Öebbi, acali s akked trusi s. Mass iw, s tidep, Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu".

# 1515

Icula yissen, di lemwao anect idurar. Issawel Nuê i mmi s, i illan weêdes: "a mmi ali d yidne$, ur teppiliv ar ijehliyen"!

# 1516

Inna: "ûûôan iw d adrar, ad iyi isellek seg waman". Inna: "assa, ulac leslak si lameô n Öebbi, siwa i win i$ef Iêun". Âaddant lemwao garasen. Iûebê ed seg wid ipwa$emqen.

# 1517

Nnan: "a tamurt, seblaâ aman im, a yigenni eûûfu". Aman zzren. Iûaô lameô: irs $ef Loudi. Iffe$ uberraê: akin agdud imednas!

# 1518

Inuj Nuê ar Mass is, inna: "a Mass iw! Ni$ mmi n twacult iw. Ih, lemâahda K d tidep, Keçç Tifev akw imêaddan".

# 1519

Inna: "a Nuê! Neppa, s tidep, ur illi n wacult ik. Ih, neppa ur ixdim ayen ilhan. Ihi, ur iyI d steqsay $ef wayen ur tessinev. Nek a k Ssakwaye$, ur teppiliv seg wid ur nessin".

# 1520

Inna: "a Mass iw! Ili di lâawen iw, iwakken ur K id steqsaye$ $ef wayen ur ssine$. Ma ur iyi Tsemmêev, ur Têunev felli, ad ili$ seg imexsuôen".

# 1521

Nnan d: "a Nuê! Ers ed s tifrat s$uône£, akked lbaôaka, fellak akw $ef leoyus i illan yidek. Kra n legyus, a ten N$it. Sinna, fellasen s$uône£, aâaqeb aqeôêan".

# 1522

Tagi si teqûivin n tbavnit, Nweêêa yak tent. Ur tent tessinev, keçç, ne$ agdud ik, uqbel wagi. Ihi, eûbeô, taggara, war ccekk, i wid ipêezziben.

# 1523

I Âad, gmat sen Hud, inna: "a yagdud iw! Âabdet Öebbi! Ur tesâim ôebbi, war Neppa. Kunwi tesnulfuyem d kan.

# 1524

A yagdud iw! Ur awen ssuture$ taqdiât $ef waya. Taqdiât iw ar Win kan, iyi d Ixelqen. Day ur tefhimem ara?

# 1525

A yagdud iw! Ssutret ssmaê i Mass nnwen, sinna, steôoâet aS. Ad awen d Isse$li ageffur d ihedman, ad awen irnu tazmert i tezmert nnwen. Ur ppu$alet d ibe$wviyen".

# 1526

# 1527

war Neppa. Ihi, andit iyi akken ma tellam, sinna ur iyi sganayet.

# 1530

Ma wexxôen, ni$ ssawve$ awen d ayen i$ef id ppuceggâa$ $uôwen. A d Inûef, Mass iw, agdud war kunwi. Ur T teîîuôum s wacemma. Mass iw, s tidep, d Amêareb n yal cci".

# 1531

Mi d iusa lameô nne£, Nsellek Hud akked wid iumnen yides, s uêunu s$uône£. Nsellek iten seg uâaqeb uwâiô.

# 1532

# 1533

A ten ivfeô xezzu di ddunit agi, u deg wass n tnekra. Day, war ccekk, ur jhilen ara Âad, ar Mass nnsen? Day maççi: "akin Âad, agdud n Hud"?

# 1534

I Tamud, gmat sen ÛüÜaliê, inna: "a yagdud iw! Âabdet Öebbi! Ur tesâim ôebbi, war Neppa. Neppa Ixelq ikwen seg wakal, Izzde$ ikwen fellas. Ssutret aS ssmaê, sinna, steôoâet aS. Mass iw, s tidep, Iqeôb ed, Ippara d awal.

# 1535

Nnan as: "a Üaliê, ni$ telliv garane$, uqbel aya, d asirem nne$. Day ad a$ tekksev aâbad n wayen âabden imezwura nne$? Nekwni, s tidep, aql a$ di ccekk imcebbwel, $ef wayen u$uô la $ tneccdev".

# 1536

Inna: "a yagdud iw! Acu twalam ma ddi$ d ubeggen n Mass iw? Ifka yi d aêunu s$uôeS. Acu ara yi isellken seg ufus n Öebbi, ma aâûa$ $uôeS? Iyi ternam, siwa taxessaôt.

# 1537

A yagdud iw! Tagi d tal$wemt n Öebbi, d assekni i kunwi. Eooet ep a ppeks di tmurt n Öebbi. Ur p pjeyyifet, mulac a kwen id isami uâaqeb iqeôben".

# 1538

# 1539

Mi d iusa lameô nne£, Nsellek Üaliê akked wid iumnen yides, s uêunu s$uône£, si ddell n wass nni. Ih, Mass ik d Uohid, d Uzmir.

# 1540

Asu$u iwwet wid idensen, gwran d d imeslax deg ixxamen nnsen,

# 1541

amzun ur rbiêen degsen. Day, s tidep, ur jhilen ara Tamud, ar Mass nnsen? Day maççi: "akin Tamud"?

# 1542

Ni$ usan d imceggâen nne£ ar Ibôahim, s ubecceô. Nnan: "tifrat"! Inna: "tifrat"! Ur iâaîîel ara ibbwi d aâjmi icwin.

# 1543

Mi iwala ifassen nnsen ur d ééilen ara $uôes, isêassef iten, iugad iten. Nnan: "ur ppagwad, nekwni neppuceggaâ ed ar ugdud n Luî".

# 1544

Tameîîut is tbedd, tevûa. Nbecceô ip s Isêaq, akked Yaâqub, deffir Isêaq.

# 1545

# 1546

# 1547

# 1548

# 1549

# 1550

Mi usan imceggâen nne£ ar Luî, innu$ben, ur isâi i$il a ten ifukk. Inna: "wagi d ass uwâiô".

# 1551

# 1552

# 1553

# 1554

# 1555

Mi d iusa lameô nne£, Nesredm ip. Nesse$li d fellas abruri n yiéôa ibelbaven n talaxt.

# 1556

# 1557

I Madian, gmat sen Cuâayeb, inna: "a yagdud iw! Âabdet Öebbi! Ur tesâim ôebbi, war Neppa. Ur ssenqaset di lkil akked lmizan. Nek, wala$ kwen teôwam, u ugade$ fellawen aâaqeb, ass itezzin.

# 1558

# 1559

# 1560

# 1561

Inna: "a yagdud iw! Acu twalam, ma ddi$ d ubeggen n Mass iw? I$at iyi yis, l$it imaânen. Ur b$i$ a kwen mgirrde$, siwa $ef wayen i wen gedle$. B$i$ kan, s wayen zemre$, ad awen ûegme$ tikli. Lâawen iw s$uô Öebbi kan. Ppekle$ fellaS, utube$ T.

# 1562

A yagdud iw! Awer kwen teppara nnmara w d ibe$wviyen, a ppevôu yidwen akken tevôa d ugdud n Nuê, ne$ win n Hud, ne$ win n Üaliê! Agdud n Luî, ur ibâad ara segwen.

# 1564

# 1565

# 1566

# 1567

Mi d iusa lameô nne£, Nsellek Cuâayeb akked wid iumnen yides, s uêunu s$uône£. Asu$u iwwet wid idensen, gwran d d imeslax deg ixxamen nnsen,

amzun ur rbiêen degsen. Day maççi: "akin Madian"! Am: "akin Tamud"?

# 1569

$uô Ferâun akked imvebbôen is. Ddan d lameô n Ferâun. Lameô n Ferâun ur illi d uûwib.

# 1571

# 1573

Ayagi, si teqûivin n temdinin, i k d Nessawal. Garasent tid ibedden, tid ipwamegren.

# 1574

Ur ten Nednis. Maca, densen iman nnsen. Ur ten nefâan s wacemma, iôebbiten nnsen i la naâôen, war Öebbi, mi d iusa lameô n Mass ik. I sen rnan, siwa ssxev.

# 1575

Akka tiyta n Mass ik. Mi Iwwet timdinin i idensen, s tidep, tiyta S teqôeê, teqseê.

# 1576

# 1577

A t Neswexxeô kan ar lajel iuran.

# 1578

Ass ideg ara d ias, ur d ipmeslay yiwen, siwa ma s tesriê iS. Ad ilin igeswaêen, isaâdiyen.

# 1579

Wanag igeswaêen ad ilin di tmes, s unazaâ d imeîîi,

# 1580

ad wekkôen dinna, ayen ara dumen tmurt akked igenwan, siwa ma ur Irad ara Mass ik. Ih, Mass ik Ixeddem ayen i S ihwan.

# 1581

Wanag isaâdiyen, di Loennet, ad wekkôen, dinna, ayen ara dumen tmurt akked igenwan, siwa ma ur Irad ara Mass ik. D tikci n war tilas.

# 1582

Ur k ikeççem ccekk $ef wayen âabden widak. Ayen âabden am wayen âabden imezwura nnsen, zik. War ccekk, ad asen Nefk amur nnsen, ur inqis.

# 1583

Ni$, s tidep, Nefka Tazmamt i Musa. Mgarraden fellas. Lemmer ur d izwar ara wawal s$uô Mass ik, yili useyyi garasen. Haaten, ih, di ccekk imcebbwel fellas.

# 1584

War ccekk, akken ma llan, ad Ikafi Mass ik igiten nnsen, s lmizan. Neppa, s tidep, Issen ayen xeddmen.

# 1585

Ihi, ili d uwqim, akken i k ippunefk lameô, keçç akked wid isteôoâen yidek. Ur be$wvet. Neppa, s tidep, Ipwali ay txeddmem.

# 1586

Ur pqeôôibet ar wid idensen, a kwen tnal tmes! Ur tesâim bab, war Öebbi, ihi, ur tepwasellkem.

# 1587

èéal ûbeê, tameddit, kra n lewqat n yiv. S tidep, ise$iyen neqqven tucmitin. Ayagi d asmekti i wid ismektayen.

# 1588

Eûbeô! Öebbi, s tidep, ur Iveggiâ taqdiât n lâuûam.

# 1589

A lemmer llan, di tsuta i kwen id izwaren, imezgiyen ineqqven asefsed di tmurt! Qlilit kan seg wid Nsellek segsen. Wid idensen ddan akked wayen i ten izhan, u$alen d ibe$wviyen.

# 1592

# 1593

# 1595

# 1597

Alô. Wigi d issekniyen n Tazmamt ipbegginen.

# 1598

# 1599

Nekwni Nêekku yak tiêkayin igerzen mavi, deg wayen i k Nweêêa di Leqwôan agi, xas telliv, uqbel is, seg wid istehzan.

# 1600

Mi inna Yusef i baba s: "a baba! Nek wala$ mrawyan itran, iîij, akked waggur, wala$ ten knan iyi".

# 1601

Inna: "a mmi! Ur êekku ayen twalav i watmaten ik, ad ak andin ticeôkep. Cciîan, s tidep, d acengu n ûûeê n umdan.

# 1602

Akka, a k Ifren Mass ik, u ak Isselmed asefru n temsal, u ad Itim l$it iS, i keçç akked twacult n Yaâqub, akken it Itam, zik, af lejdud ik: Ibôahim akked Isêaq. Mass ik, s tidep, d Amusnaw, d Uûwib".

# 1603

Ni$, di Yusef akked watma s, illa ussekni i wid isteqsayen.

# 1604

Mi nnan: "war ccekk, ifen a$, Yusef akked gma s, akken iten iêemmel babat nne$, u nekwni d îîeôma. Babat nne$, s tidep, haat di ttelfan n ûûeê.

# 1605

En$et Yusef, ne$ nfut ep si tmurt, a d ilhu degwen babat wen, sinna, a ppu$alem d imdanen ixeddmen ayen ilhan".

# 1606

Inna win d immeslayen, degsen: "ur neqqet Yusef, veggôet ep ar lqaâa n wannu. Ma tgam akka, a t iddem yiwen umsebrid".

# 1607

Nnan: "a babat nne$, acu k iu$en, ur a$ tuminev ara, $ef Yusef. Nekwni, fellas, s tidep, d unûiêen.

# 1608

Sseddu t yidne$ azekka, ad izhu, ad iurar. Nekwni, war ccekk, a nêareb fellas".

# 1609

# 1610

# 1611

Mi t bbwin, mwafaqen a t rôen ar lqaâa n wannu, Nweêêa yas: "ad asen temlev, s tidep, lameô agi nnsen, nitni ur éôin".

# 1612

U$alen d tameddit, ar babat sen, pprun.

# 1613

# 1614

Bbwin d tasedrit is, degs idamen n rrya. Inna: "xaîi! D iman nnwen i wen d iccacven lameô. Ilha ûûbeô. Anuju $eô Öebbi, mgal ayen d teêkam".

# 1615

Usan d iminigen, uznen win id ippagwmen, issader ssvel is. Inna: "a lxiô, wagi d aqcic"! Ffren t, amzun d sselâa. Öebbi Iéôa acu xeddmen.

# 1616

Zzenzen t, s ôôxa, s kra iûuôdiyen. Ur as fkin ara azal.

# 1617

Inna, i tmeîîut is, Umaûôi i t iu$en: "eôêeb yis, amar ad a$ infaâ, at nerr d mmit nne$". Akka ay Nesseqâad Yusef di tmurt, iwakken ad as Nesseêfev asefru n temsal. Öebbi d Amezwaru s lameô iS, maca tegwti n medden ur éôin ara.

# 1618

Mi d immeêtel, Nefka yas ûûwab, tussna. Akka ay Nepkafi iâaôviyen.

# 1619

Teb$a t tin u$ur izde$. Terra tibbura, u tenna: "eyya keçç"! Inna: "ad iyi Ineooi Öebbi! Ni$ bab iw iôêeb yissi. S tidep, ur rebêen imednas".

# 1620

S tidep, teb$a t, u neppa ib$a p, lemmer ur iwala ara atebbet n Mass is. Akka, iwakken a Nessebâad fellas tuccva, lâaô. Neppa, s tidep, seg imdanen nne£ izedganen.

# 1621

Uzzlen ar tebburt, tcerreg as tasedrit is, si zdeffir. Mmugren, argaz is, ar tebburt. Tenna: "acu ay d aqeîîi n win iâabwlen ad iccmet tawacult ik, siwa lêebs ne$ aâaqeb aqeôêan"?

# 1622

Inna: "d neppat iyi ib$an". Icuhhed ed yiwen unagi si twacult is: "ma teqqeôs tsedrit si zdat, tenna d tidep, u neppa d akeddab.

# 1623

Ma teqqeôs tsedrit si zdeffir, teskaddeb, u neppa seg at tidep".

# 1624

Mi iwala teqqeôs tsedrit si zdeffir, inna: "ayagi, war ccekk, si nncub nnkwent. Ih, nncub nnkwent d timeqwôaêanin.

# 1625

A Yusef, ppu ayagi, u kem ssuter ssmaê ubekkav im. Kem, s tidep, teccvev".

# 1626

La qqaôent tlawin, di temdint: "tameîîut umdebbeô têemmel acrik is. Teshebl ip tayri. F akken nwala, appan, s tidep, di ttelfan n ûûeê".

# 1627

Mi tesla s nncub nnsent, tuzen $uôsent, thegga yasent tanalt. I yal yiwet segsent, tefka tafrut. Tenna: "effe$ ed garasent". Mi t walant, isdehc itent, jerêent ifassen nnsent, nnant: "êaca Öebbi, wagi maççi d amdan, wagi siwa d lmelk ukyis".

# 1628

Tenna: "d wagi i$ef iyi tlummemt. Ih, b$i$ t, neppa iqqim zeddig. Ma ur ixdim ara ay s umôe$, war ccekk, ad ipwaêbes, ad ipwaêqeô".

# 1629

Inna: "a Mass iw! Smenyafe$ lêebs i wayen u$ur iyi d ssawalent. Ma ur Tesbaâdev ara felli nncub nnsent, ad male$ $uôsent, ad ili$ seg wid ur nessin".

# 1630

Ijaweb as d Mass is. Issebâad fellas nncub nnsent. Neppa, s tidep, Issel, d Amusnaw.

# 1631

Sinna, mi ten usan issekniyen, ufan, war ccekk, ilaq a t irr ar lêebs, kra n tallit.

# 1632

Kecmen yides, ar lêebs, sin ilmeéiyen. Inna yiwen degsen: "nek wala$ iman iw, la teééme$ ccôab". Inna d wayev: "nek wala$ iman iw, la ppawi$ a$ôum $ef uqeôôu w, la teppen segs ifrax. Ssefru ya$ p id. Ih, nwala k seg iâaôviyen".

# 1633

Inna: "seg wayen iyi ss$eô Mass iw, ad awen p id ssefru$, uqbel a kwen id iawev lqut i wen ppakken. Nek ooi$ ddin n ugdud ur numin s Öebbi, u nitni nekôen laxeôt.

# 1634

Ddi$ d ddin n lejdud iw: Ibôahim, Isêaq akked Yaâqub. Ur a$ ippunefk a nezdukkel acemma i Öebbi. Ayagi si lfevl n Öebbi fellane$, akw $ef imdanen. Maca, tegwti n yimdanen ur snemmiren.

# 1635

A yimeddukwal iw n lêebs, menyif imawlan imfaôaqen, ne$ Öebbi Yiwen, Aqehhaô?

# 1636

Ay tâabdem, war Neppa, d ismawen kan i sen tefkam, kunwi akked imezwura nnwen. Ur asen d Issers ara Öebbi kra udabu. Lêukm ar Öebbi kan. Iumeô ed ur tâabdem, siwa Neppa. D wagi ay d ddin uûwib, maca tegwti n yimdanen ur ssinen.

# 1637

A yimeddukwal iw n lêebs, wanag yiwen degwen ad ismiri ccôab, i bab is, wayev ad ippusemmeô $ef umidag, ifrax ad nneqben aqeôôu s. Ippuseyya lameô $ef wayen iyi d testeqsam".

# 1638

Inna i win iêûa ad islek, segsen: "ar bab ik, smekti iyi d". Cciîan iseppu t, ur t id ismekti ar bab is. Irna, di lêebs, kra iseggwasen.

# 1639

Inna ugellid: "nek wala$ ûa testan tiqebwaniyin, la tent teppent ûa tuvâifin, akked ûa tyedrin tizegzawin, tiyav d tiqquôanin. A yimvebbôen, ssefrut iyi d targit, ma tellam seg wid issefruyen tirga".

# 1640

Nnan: "d tirga iwlellsen. Ur nelli d imusnawen i usefru n tirga".

# 1641

Win i isellken si sin nni, armi tallit id immekti, inna: "nek, ad awen d awi$ asefru ines, aznet iyi.

# 1642

A Yusef, bab n tidep, ssefru ya$ d: ûa testan tiqebwaniyin, la tent teppent ûa tuvâifin, akked ûa tyedrin tizegzawin, tiyav d tiqquôanin. Amar, ma u$ale$ ar imdanen, amar ad éôen".

# 1643

Inna: "zerâat ûa iseggwasen imyevfaôen. Ayen tzerâam, eooet ep di tyedrin is, siwa cwiî ara teççem.

# 1644

Sinna, deffir sen, a d asen ûa iwaâôen. Ad ççen ayen i sen theggam siwa cwiî, seg wayen txeznem.

# 1645

Sinna a d ias, deffir waya, useggwas n tallalt i medden, ideg ara éden".

# 1646

Inna ugellid: "awit ep id $uôi". Mi t id iusa umersul, inna: "u$al ar bab ik, u steqsi t acu ay d l$eôv n tlawin i ijerêen ifassen nnsent. Mass iw, s tidep, Issen nncub nnsent".

# 1647

Inna: "acu ara d tinimt mi teb$amt Yusef"? Nnant: "êaca Öebbi, ur nufi $uôes tuccva". Tenna d tmeîîut umvebbeô: "tura, a d tban tidep. D nek i t ib$an, ma d neppa, s tidep, d bab n tidep".

# 1648

"Akka, iwakken ad iéeô ur t xdiâa$ ara s tuffra. Öebbi ur Inehhu nncub n lxeyyan.

# 1649

Ur pzekki$ iman iw. Tanefsit, s tidep, tezzu$uô ar tuccva, siwa ma Iêun Mass iw. Mass iw, s tidep, Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu".

# 1650

Inna ugellid: "awit ep id $uôi, d laâtiq iw". Mi s immeslay, inna: "keçç, assa, nefka yak adabu, laman".

# 1651

Inna: "wekkel iyi $ef lemxazen n tmurt, nek d amêareb amusnaw".

# 1652

Akka ay Nesseqâad Yusef di tmurt, ad izde$ anda i s ihwa. Nepêunu $ef win i £ ihwan, ur Nesôuêu arraz iâaôviyen.

# 1653

S tidep, arraz n laxeôt yif it, i wid iumnen u llan pêezziben.

# 1654

Usan watmaten n Yusef, kecmen $uôes, iâqel iten, nitni ur t âqilen.

# 1655

Mi sen ifka ppâabgat nnsen, inna: "awit iyi d gmat wen s babat wen. Day ur twalam ara zade$ awen lkil, u, nek, ife$ akw wid isnebgaten?

# 1656

Ma ur iyi t id tebbwim ara, ur awen nepktili $uôi, ur iyi d tepsamim ".

# 1657

Nnan: "a nêawet baba s fellas; akka ara nexdem".

# 1658

Inna i iqeddacen is: "rret selâa nnsen deg icekkaôen nnsen, amar a p âaqlen mara awven ar twacult nnsen, amar a d u$alen".

# 1659

Mi bbwven ar babat sen, nnan: "a babat nne$, igdel fella$ lkil, azen gmat nne$ yidne$, iwakken a d nektil. Nekwni, war ccekk, a nêareb fellas".

# 1660

Inna: "day a kwen amne$ fellas, akken i kwen umne$, zik, $ef gma s? Öebbi Yif akw imêaraben. Neppa Iphunu sennig akw iêninen".

# 1661

Mi ldin lqecc nnsen, ufan tu$al iten id selâa nnsen. Nnan: "a babat nne$, ur neb$i tagi, selâa nne$ tu$al a$ d. A d nessikrer i twacult nne$, a nêareb $ef gmat nne$, a d nernu ppâabga n ul$wem. Tagi d ppâabga tushilt".

# 1662

Inna: "ur t sedduye$ yidwen, d awez$i, siwa ma tcubkem iyi s Öebbi, ard a yi t id terrem, siwa ma zzin awen". Mi s âahden, inna: "Öebbi d Awkil $ef wayen id nenna".

# 1663

Inna: "a tarwa, ur keççmet si yiwet n tebburt, kecmet si tebbura imgarraden. Ula i wen xedme$, bippa, ar loiha n Öebbi. Aêuddu siwa win n Öebbi. FellaS ppekle$, fellaS ay ppeklen wid ippkalen".

# 1664

Mi kecmen akken i sen iumeô babat sen, ula i sen ixdem, bippa, ar loiha n Öebbi. D ayen ilezmen kan i iseyya Yaqub, deg iman is. Neppa, s tidep, isâa tamusni i s Nesselmed, maca tegwti n yimdanen ur ssinen.

# 1665

Mi kecmen ar Yusef, ibbwi gma s $uôes, inna: "nekkini d gma k, ur $webbel $ef wayen xeddmen".

# 1666

Mi sen ifka ppâabgat nnsen, irra taqbuct deg ucekkaô n gma s. Sinna, iberreê uberraê: "a yat terkaf, kunwi, war ccekk, d imakwaren"!

# 1667

Nnan, u zzin $uôsen: "d acu tesôuêem"?

# 1668

Nnan: "nesôuê taqbuct ugellid. Win ip id ibbwin, ad as nefk ppâabga n ul$wem. Nek, vemne$ t".

# 1669

Nnan: "s Öebbi, nni$ teéôam ur d nusa ara a nessefsed tamurt, ur nelli d imakwaren".

# 1670

Nnan: "d acu ay d aqeîîi s, ma teskadbem"?

# 1671

Nnan: " aqeîîi n win i p ibbwin di tcekkaôt is, d yiman is. Akka ay nepkafi imednas".

# 1672

Ibda la ipqellib icekkaôen, uqbel win n gma s, sinna, issuffe$ ip id seg ucekkaô n gma s. Akka ay Nefka ticeôkep i Yusef. Ur izmir ad iîîef gma s, s lqanun ugellid, siwa ma Irad Öebbi. Nessalay, tiseddaôin, win i £ihwan. Sennig bu tussna, illa Umusnaw.

# 1673

Nnan: "ma iuker, ni$ iuker, zik, yiwen n watma s". Iffer ip Yusef $uôes, ur asen p id inna ara. Inna: "aql akwen deg yir êala. Öebbi Yif akw akken Iéôa ayen d teqqaôem".

# 1674

Nnan: "a yameqwôan, baba s, s tidep, wesser. Eîîef yiwen segne$ deg umekkan is. Nwala k, ih, telliv si lâuûam".

# 1675

Inna: "ur a$ Iâammed Öebbi a neîîef, siwa win u$uô nufa ta$awsa nne$. Mulac, war ccekk, a nili d imednas".

# 1676

Mi uysen segs, mcawaôen, inna umeqwôan segsen: "day ur teéôim ara, ar babat wen tcubkem t s Öebbi, u, zik, tveggâam Yusef? Ihi, ur pôuêu$ si tmurt a, d awez$i, alamma iserreê iyi baba, ne$ Ifra Öebbi felli. Neppa, Yif akw imêaddan.

# 1677

U$alet ar babat wen, tinem as: a babat nne$, mmi k, s tidep, iuker. Ncehhed kan $ef wayen neéôa, ur nessawev i tbavnit.

# 1678

Steqsi tamdint ideg i nella, akked terkift ukud nedda. Ih, d tidep, ay d nenna".

# 1679

Inna: "xaîi! Lameô seg iman nnwen. Ilha ûûbeô. Amar Öebbi a yi ten id Iawi akw. Neppa, s tidep, d Bab n ûûwab, d Amusnaw".

# 1680

Ijuneb iten, u inna: "a lêif iw $ef Yusef"! Allen is ijegger itent u$ilif, innu$ben.

# 1681

Nnan: "s Öebbi, tezgiv tesmektayev d Yusef, alamma tu$alev d amuvin, ne$ seg wid immuten".

# 1682

Inna: "la pcetki$ kan i Öebbi, s uneémi w akked u$wbel iw. Ssne$, s$uô Öebbi, ayen ur tessinem.

# 1683

A yarraw iw, ôuêet, steqsit $ef Yusef akked gma s. Ur ppayset di tecvaî n Öebbi. Ih, i ippaysen di tecvaî n Öebbi, siwa agdud ijehliyen".

# 1684

Mi bbwven $uôes, nnan as: "a yameqwôan, nekwni akked twacult nne$, nepwa$. Nusa d s selâa ôxisen, semd as lkil, seddeq a$. Öebbi, s tidep, Ipkafi wid ipseddiqen".

# 1685

Inna: "teéôam i tgam i Yusef akked gma s, mi kunwi, d wid ur nessin"?

# 1686

Nnan: "keçç, s tidep, maççi d Yusef "? Inna: "nek d Yusef, atan gma. Ni$ I$at a$ Öebbi. Ih, wid ipêezziben, wid iûebbôen ... Öebbi, s tidep, ur Isôuêu arraz iâaôviyen".

# 1687

Nnan: "s Öebbi ar k Ismenyaf Öebbi garane$. Nekwni, s tidep, neccev".

# 1688

Inna: "ur telli tiyta degwen, assa. Ad awen Isemmeê Öebbi! Neppa Yif akw wid ipêunun.

# 1689

Awit tasedrit iw agi, erret ep $ef udem n baba, ad iêlu yiéôi s. Aset ed $uôi, s twacult nnwen, meôôa".

# 1690

Mi teqlaâ terkift, babat sen ibda la iqqaô: "nek, s tidep, sraêe$ rriêa n Yusef, awi d kan ur teqqaôem ara: la isxeôwiv".

# 1691

Nnan: "s Öebbi, ar k mazal di ttelfan ik n zik".

# 1692

Mi d iusa ubcir, issers as p $ef udem is, llint ed wallen is, inna: "day ur awen nni$ ara: nek ssne$, s$uô Öebbi, ayen ur tessinem"?

# 1693

Nnan as: "a babat nne$, ssuter ad a$ pwasemmêen ibekkaven nne$. S tidep, nella d imednab".

# 1694

Inna: "deqqal ad ssutre$, i Mass iw, ad awen Isemmeê. Neppa, s tidep, Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu".

# 1695

Mi bbwven ar Yusef, isteôêeb s imawlan is. Inna: "kecmet ar Maseô, di laman, ma Irad Öebbi".

# 1696

Issuli imawlan is ar usgeld. £lin, knan as. Inna: "a baba! D wagi ay d asefru n targit iw, n zik. Ni$ Issuffe$ ip Mass iw! Ni$ Iga yi leqôaô mi yi d Issuffe$ si lêebs. Ikkes ikwen id si sseêôa, deffir tismin i isker Cciîan, gari d watma. Mass iw, s tidep, d Laîif i win i S ihwan. Ih, Neppa d Amusnaw, d Bab n ûûwab.

# 1697

A Mass iw, ni$ Tefkiv iyi si tgelda, Tesêefvev iyi asefru n temsal. Axellaq n tmurt akked igenwan, Keçç, d Bab iw di ddunit, di laxeôt, Eddem ôôuê iw d amvua, Ssiwev iyi ar wid imaânen".

# 1698

Tagi, si teêkayin n tbavnit, Nweêêa yak p in. Ur telliv $uôsen, mi mwafaqen a p andin.

# 1699

Tegwti n yimdanen, xas tâapbev, ur ppamnen.

# 1700

Ur asen ssutur kra n teqdiât. Neppa, d asmekti kan i imavalen.

# 1701

I illan deg issekniyen di tmurt akked igenwan! La teddun fellasen, maca wexxôen asen.

# 1702

Tegwti, segsen, ur ppamnen s Öebbi, siwa ma curken.

# 1703

Day ppeklen ur asen isburru yara uâaqeb n Öebbi, ne$ ur ten id ippas ara yimir, deqzalla, ur pfaqan?

# 1704

Ini: "wagi d abrid iw, la pnuju$ ar Öebbi ad Ildi allen, i nek akked wid iddan yidi. Gedha s Öebbi! Ur lli$ seg wid ipcaraken".

# 1705

Nuzen ed kan, uqbel ik, irgazen seg imezda$ n temdinin, iwumi Nweêêa. Day ur unagen ara di tmurt, ad walin amek tevôa d wid i ten id izwaren? Ih, pifxiô axxam aneggaru i wid ipêezziben. Day ur tefhimem ara?

# 1706

Alamma, mi uysen imazanen, u meyyzen ar skaddben ten, tusa ten id tallalt s$uône£. Nepsellik win i £ ihwan. Ur ipwakkas ara ssxev nne£, i ugdud ibe$wviyen.

# 1707

Ni$, di teêkayin nnsen, illa uselmed i yuâqilen. Ur telli d awal id innulfan. Neppat tetebbet ed ay d izwaren, tfeûûel ed yal cci. D nnhaya u d aêunu i ugdud iumnen.

# 1708

Almô. Wigi d issekniyen n Tezmamt. Ayen i k d irsen, s$uô Mass ik, d tidep, maca tegwti n medden ur ppamnen.

# 1709

Öebbi i Issulin igenwan war tigwejda ara twalim, sinna, Iâannec $ef usgeld. Iêeppem i yiîij d waggur ad ddun, akw, ar lajel ipwassnen. Iseyyi lameô, Ipfeûûil issekniyen, amar a pepputebbtem $ef temlilit d Mass nnwen.

# 1710

Neppa i Isswesâen tamurt. Irra degs idurar, isaffen. Irra tayuga di yal ppemôa. Ip$ummu ass s yiv. Deg waya, s tidep, d issekniyen i ugdud ipxemmimen.

# 1711

Di tmurt, tibêirin tioiratin, leonanat n téuôin, nnaâma, tizdayin, v$an ne$ ur v$in, cerken aman nnsen. Nesmenyaf kra i kra, i wuççi. Deg waya, s tidep, d issekniyen i ugdud ifehmen.

# 1712

Ma twehmev, issewham ay d qqaôen: "ma nu$al d akal, day fella$, s tidep, lxelq amaynut"? D wigi i inekôen Mass nnsen. Wigi, azaglu $ef tmegôav. Wigi d at tmes, nitni, degs, ad wekkôen.

# 1713

Sêaren k ar tucmip, uqbel ise$. Ni$ vôant am tigi, uqbel nnsen. Mass ik, s tidep, $uôeS ssmaê i imdanen deg wayen ccven. Mass ik, s tidep, Iwâaô deg uâaqeb.

# 1714

La qqaôen wid ijehlen: "a lemmer id irs $uôes ussekni, s$uô Mass is". Keçç, d aneddaô kan. I yal agdud, win inehhun.

# 1715

Öebbi Iéôa i illan di yal tadist, amek teddun inzikmiren. Yal cci, $uôeS, s lmizan.

# 1716

Amusnaw n wayen iffren akked wayen ur neffir. Ameqwôan, Aâlayan.

# 1717

Iâuva segwen win i$emven awal, d win it iberêen, win iffren deg iv, d win d ivehôen deg wass.

# 1718

Isâa iâssasen zdat es, deffir es, pêaraben fellas, s lameô n Öebbi. Öebbi, s tidep, ur Ipbeddil i illan deg ugdud, alamma bedlen i illan deg iman nnsen. Ma Irad Öebbi ayen n dir, i ugdud, ur t itekkes yiwen. Ur sâin amâiwen, war Neppa.

# 1719

D Neppa i wen d Ippawin lebôaq, degs tugdi, asirem. Isskar ed asigna aéayan.

# 1720

Tesbuccuâ aS termegt, s ccekôan, akken lmalayek, seg wakken ugadent eP. Ippazen ed ssiâqat, Ipêaz yisent win i S ihwan. Nitni pnamaren $ef Öebbi. Neppa teqseê tezmert iS.

# 1721

£uô Neppa, anuju n tidep. Wid u$uô la pnujun, war Neppa, ur asen d pparan s wacemma. Am win issendin ifassen i waman, ib$a ad awven s imi s, ur ibbwiv ar leb$i s. Anuju ijehliyen ar ttelfan kan.

# 1722

I Öebbi la kennun wid illan di tmurt akked igenwan, b$an ne$ ugin, akked tili nnsen, taûebêit, tameddit.

# 1723

Ini: "anwa ay d Mass n tmurt akked igenwan"? Ini: "d Öebbi. Ihi day a pperrem d iêbiben, war Neppa, wid ur nemlik, i yiman nnsen, aba$uô ne$ vveôô"? Ini: "day iaâdel uder$al akked win ipwalin? Ne$, day âadlent tillas akked tafat? Ne$, rran imcurak i Öebbi, i ixelqen am lxelq iS, ufan t ippemcabi"? Ini: "d Öebbi i Ixelqen yal cci. D Neppa ay d Yiwen, d Aqehhaô".

# 1724

Isse$lay ed aman, seg igenni. Serrun deg $ezôan, s leqdeô nnsen. Acercuô ippawi ikuftan ippifliwen. Ppemcabin ikuftan ar wayen fessin di tmes, iwakken ad ûenâen ôôêuê ne$ dduzan. Akka ay d Isskan Öebbi tidep akked tkerkas. Ihi ikuftan ad ppuveggôen, ma d wayen inefâen medden, a d igwri di tmurt. Akka ay d Ippak Öebbi imedyaten.

# 1725

Lfayeq i wid ijawben i Mass nnsen. Wid ur aS njaweb ara, xas ad sâun i illan akw di tmurt, berdayen, ur ten id ifeddu. I widak, leêsab adiran. Axxam nnsen d Loahennama. A tanezdu$t tucmip!

# 1726

Day win iéôan ar ayen i k d irsen, s$uô Mass ik, d tidep, am win idre$len? Siwa uâqilen id ismektayen.

# 1727

Wid iîîfen di laâqed n Öebbi, ur pôuéun nnesba.

# 1728

Wid issemlilen ayen id Iumeô Öebbi ad imlil, u ppagwaden Mass nnsen, u ppagwaden aqeîîi adiran.

# 1729

Wid iûebôen, ssaramen udem n Mass nnsen, bedden i téallit, pseddiqen seg wayen is iten N$at, s tuffra u âinâni, swexxiôen tucmip s yise$. I nitni, agwav s Axxam.

# 1730

Leonanat n Âaden ara kecmen, akked wid ixeddmen ayen ilhan, seg ibabaten nnsen, si tlawin nnsen, si tarwa nnsen. Lmalayek a d ppasent $uôsen si yal tabburt.

# 1731

Tifrat fellawen, ilmend n wayen tûebôem! D asaâdi, wagwav s Axxam!

# 1732

Wid ipôuéun laâqed n Öebbi, deffir lemwafaqa s, wid igezmen ayen d Iumeô Öebbi ad imlil, u ssefsaden di tmurt, wigi, i nitni xezzu, i nitni yir axxam.

# 1733

Öebbi Issugut ôôeéq i win i S ihwan, u Iwezzen. Taâoeb iten tmeddurt n ddunit. Tameddurt n ddunit, d urar kan, zdat laxeôt.

# 1734

La qqaôen wid ijehlen: "a lemmer id iris, $uôes, ussekni s$uô Mass is"! Ini: "Öebbi, s tidep, Itellif win i S ihwan. Inehhu $uôeS, wid isteôoiâen,

# 1735

wid iumnen, iwumi itheddin wul, mara d mmektin Öebbi". Ni$, s usmekti n Öebbi, pheddinen wulawen.

# 1736

Ssaâd, akked taggara igerzen, i wid iumnen, ixeddmen ayen ilhan.

# 1737

Akka ay k id Nuzen, i lois id zwaren leoyus, ad asen temlev, ayen ik d Nweêêa. Nitni jehlen $uô Uênin. Ini: "Neppa d Mass iw, ur illi ôebbi siwa Neppa; ppekle$ fellaS, asteôoaâ iw $uôeS".

# 1738

A lemmer kan Leqwôan isselêa idurar, iceqqeq tamurt, ne$ issenîeq ed lmeggtin! Xaîi! Lumuô akw i Öebbi. Day ur éôin ara wid iumnen, ar, ma ihwa yaS, Öebbi ad Inhu medden meôôa? Zgan wid ijehlen a ten tewwet ssixîa, ilmend n wayen xeddmen. Ne$ a ppevôu ar tama n yixxamen nnsen, alamma tusa d lemâahda n Öebbi. Öebbi, s tidep, ur Ipzeggil ppaâud.

# 1739

Ni$ mmaâlken, uqbel ik, deg imazanen. Ooi$ lmudda i wid ijehlen, sinna, Ïîfe$ ten. A yaâaqeb iW imiren!

# 1740

Day Win Ibedden, ar yal amdan, $ef wayen ikseb...? Curken aS i Öebbi. Ini: "semmit asen! Ne$, ad aS temlem ayen ur Iéôi di tmurt? Ne$ d ismawen n tkerkas"? Xaîi! Wid ijehlen, âaobent pen nncub nnsen. Ppuveôôfen seg ubrid. Win Itlef Öebbi, ur isâi w ara t inhun.

# 1741

Fellasen aâaqeb, di tmeddurt n ddunit. Aâaqeb n laxert, s tidep, aâer. Ur sâin ara ten ifukken, seg ufus n Öebbi.

# 1742

Amek tga Loennet i ippuweââden i wid iêezzben: ddaw as isaffen ppazzalen, lqut is akked tili s, d imezgiyen. D tagi ay d taggara n wid iêezzben. Taggara ijehliyen, d times.

# 1743

Wid iwumi Nefka Tazmamt, ad feôêen s wayen i k d irsen. Illa wayen ugin kra ikabaren. Ini: "pwamôe$ kan ad âabde$ Öebbi, ur aS pcarake$. Pnuju$ $uôeS, tu$alin iw $uôeS".

# 1744

# 1745

Ni$ Nuzen ed imazanen, uqbel ik, Nefka yasen tilawin, tarwa. Ur ippunefk ara i umazan a d iawi assekni siwa ma Iâammed Öebbi. Yal lajel s Tezmamt is.

# 1748

# 1749

Ni$ ppandin wid i ten id izwaren. Tiêeôci, akw, ar Öebbi. Iéôa i ikseb yal iman. Ad éôen ijehliyen anwa ara iawven s Axxam.

# 1750

Qqaôen wid ijehlen: "ur telliv d amazan". Ini: "ad Iqadd Öebbi d Anagi gari yidwen, akked kra isâan tussna n Tazmamt".

# 1751

# 1755

# 1759

timuliwin: s yitran, nitni pwanhan.

# 1918

Day Win Ixelqen am win ur nxelleq? Day ur d tesmektayem ara?

# 1919

Lemmer a pêesbem l$it n Öebbi, ur tezmirem. Ih, Öebbi, war ccekk, Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu.

# 1920

Öebbi Iéôa ayen teffrem akked wayen teqqaôem.

# 1921

Wid u$uô pnujun, war Öebbi, ur illi wayen xelqen. D nitni i ipwaxelqen.

# 1922

D lmeggtin ur d imuddiren, ur éôin melmi ara ten id ssekren.

# 1923

Öebbi nnwen d Öebbi Yiwen. Wid ur numin ara s laxeôt, d ulawen nnsen i iugin. U nitni pzzuxun.

# 1924

War ccekk, Öebbi Iéôa ayen teffren, akked wayen qqaôen. Neppa, s tidep, ur Iêemmel ara imzuxiyen.

# 1925

Ma nnan asen: "d acu id Issers Mass nnwen"? Qqaôen: "d timucuha imezwura".

# 1926

Ad bibben, ass n tnekra, tiâakkwmin nnsen, s pmam nnsent, akked wumur si tâakkwmin n wid telfen, mebla ma faqen. Day maççi dir it wayen bubben?

# 1927

Ih, undin p, wid i ten id izwaren. Öebbi Iaâtad lebni nnsen, si llsas. I$li d ssqef fellasen. Iusa ten id uâaqeb seg wanda ur bnin.

# 1928

Sinna, ass n tnekra, a ten Idull, ad Yini: "anda ten icriken iW, i$ef temnamarem"? Nnan imawlan n tussna: "war ccekk, ddell akked ddens, assa, $ef ijehliyen

# 1929

iwumi ddment lmalayek leôwaê, nitni densen iman nnsen". A d ssutren tifrat: "ur nexdim kra n tucmip". Xaîi, Öebbi, s tidep, Iéôa ayen txeddmem.

# 1930

Kecmet si tebbura, ar Loahennama; degs a pwekkôem. A yicmet uxxam imzuxiyen!

# 1931

Ad inin i wid ipêezziben: "d acu id Issers Mass nnwen"? A d inin: "d lxiô". I wid imaânen, ise$ di ddunit agi. Pifxiô, war ccekk, axxam aneggaru. Ay d umâin uxxam n wid ipêezziben!

# 1932

Ad kecmen leonanat n Âaden, ddawat sen isaffen ppazzalen; degsen, i nitni, ayen i sen ihwan. Akka i Ipkafi Öebbi wid ipêezziben,

# 1933

# 1934

Day a pôaoun kan tisin n lmalayek $uôsen, ne$ a d iawev lameô n Mass ik? Akka ay xedmen imezwura nnsen. Ur ten Idnis Öebbi, maca densen iman nnsen.

# 1935

D tucmitin xeddmen, i ten iwwten. Izzi yasen wayen i$ef pmmaâliken.

# 1936

Nnan wid ipcaraken: "Lemmer i S ihwi i Öebbi, ur naâbed acemma, war Neppa, nekwni akked imezwura nne$. Ur negdel acemma, war ayen Igdel". Akka ay xedmen imezwura nnsen. Day illa wayen iwatan i Umazan, siwa awal ipbegginen?

# 1937

Ni$ Nuzen ed amazan i yal lois: "âabdet Öebbi, janbet iôebbiten n tkerkas". Garasen, llan wid Inha Öebbi; garasen, wid i$ef iura ttelfan. Iniget di tmurt, walit amek tevôa d inekkaôen.

# 1938

Xas tôe$wbev $ef nnhaya nnsen, Öebbi, s tidep, ur Inehhu wid Itlef. Ur asen illi usettaô.

# 1939

Ggulen s Öebbi, liman iûeêêan nnsen, ar ur d Ippara ara Öebbi wid immuten. Xaîi, lemâahda fellas d tidep, maca tegwti n medden ur ssinen.

# 1940

Iwakken ad asen d ibeggen ayen i$ef mgarraden, iwakken ad éôen wid ijehlen, ar nitni, war ccekk, llan d ikeddaben.

# 1941

# 1942

# 1943

wid iûebôen u ppeklen $ef Mass nnsen.

# 1944

# 1945

# 1946

Wid iundin tucmitin, aâni $ilen ur Iôemmu ara Öebbi di tmurt, ne$ ur ten id ippawev ara uâaqeb, seg wanda ur bnin?

# 1947

Ne$ ur ten id ikkat ara di cce$l nnsen, ur sfunnugen?

# 1948

Ne$ ur ten ikkat ara cwiî, cwiî. Ih, Mass nnwen, war ccekk, Issuruf, Ipêunu.

# 1949

# 1950

# 1951

Ppagwaden Mass nnsen, sennig sen, xeddmen ayen i sen ippumôen.

# 1952

# 1953

# 1954

# 1955

# 1956

# 1957

# 1958

# 1959

# 1960

# 1961

I wid ur numin ara s laxert: amedya ucmit. I Öebbi: amedya aâlayen mavi. Neppa d Uzmir, d Bab n ûûwab.

# 1962

Öebbi, lemmer Ipqissi medden, $ef ddens nnsen, ur d Ippaoa, degs, amexluq. Maca, Iswexxiô iten ar lajel ipwassnen. Ma iusa d lajel nnsen, ur t swexxiôen, ur t id seqôaben, s ssaâa.

# 1963

Garen aS d, i Öebbi, ayen keôhen. Skaddben yilsawen nnsen, mi qqaôen ar ayen ilhan, nnsen. Ay nnsen, war ccekk, d times. Ih, nitni ad zwiren.

# 1964

S Öebbi, ni$ Nuzen ed, i leoyus, uqbel ik. Cciîan icebbeê asen igiten nnsen. Assa, d bab nnsen. I nitni, aâaqeb aqeôêan.

# 1965

# 1966

# 1967

# 1968

# 1969

# 1970

# 1971

Ixelq ikwen Öebbi, sinna, ad awen Iddem ôôuê. Kra, segwen, ad ccerfeffen mavi, alamma ur ppissinen acemma mbaâd ma ssnen. Ih, Öebbi d Amusnaw, d Aêernuk.

# 1972

# 1973

Iga yawen Öebbi, seg iman nnwen, tilawin nnwen. Ifka yawen, si tlawin nnwen, arraw d warraw n warraw. Iôeéq ikwen s wayen ilhan. Day ad amnen di tkerkas, ad nekôen l$it n Öebbi?

# 1974

Âabden, war Öebbi, wid ur nesâi acemma, swayes ara ten ôeéqen, si tmurt akked igenwan, u ur zmiren.

# 1975

Ur d ppawit imedyaten i Öebbi. Ih, Öebbi Issen, kunwi ur tessinem.

# 1976

Ifka d Öebbi amedya n wakli, d ayla, ur izmir i wacemma, akked yiwen iwumi Nefka, s $uône£, ôôeéq ilhan. Ipseddiq, segs, s tuffra ne$ âinani. Day âadlen? Ccekôan i Öebbi. Maca, tegwti, segsen, ur ssinen.

# 1977

Ifka d Öebbi amedya n sin irgazen. Yiwen d agugam, ur izmir i wacemma. D taâkkwemt i bab is. Anda it iuzen, ur d ippawi lxiô. Day iaâdel akked win ippamôen lêeqq, u neppa deg ubrid uwqim?

# 1978

N Öebbi tabavnit n tmurt akked igenwan. Lameô n yimir, am unqaj n tiî kan, ne$ ur ibbwiv. Ih, Öebbi Izmer i yal cci.

# 1979

Öebbi Issuffe$ ikwen id si tâabbav n tyimmatin nnwen, ur tessinem acemma. Ifka yawen timejjin, iéôi, ul, amar a ppesnemmrem.

# 1980

Day ur walan ara ifôax, têeppem fellasen lhawa igenni, ur ten iîîif yiwen siwa Öebbi? Deg waya, s tidep, issekniyen i ugdud iumnen.

# 1981

Öebbi Irra yawen ixxamen nnwen d tanezdu$t. Irra yawen ixxamen, s igwelman n lmal nnwen. Fessusit, ass n yinig, d wass uqeggel. Taduî nnsen, ccâaô nnsen, inéaden nnsen, i leêwal akked dduzan, tallit kan.

# 1982

Deg wayen Ixleq, Öebbi Ifka yawen d tili. Irra yawen, deg idurar, ûûôanat. Ifka yawen iceîîiven i kwen isdarayen seg u$amac, iceîîiven i kwen ipfukkun si lbe$wv nnwen. Akka, ad awen Itim l$it iS. Amar a ppanzem.

# 1983

Ma wexxôen, i illan fellak, siwa awal ipbegginen.

# 1984

Âaqlen l$it n Öebbi, sinna, nekôen t. Tegwti, degsen, d ijehliyen.

# 1985

Ass ideg ara d Nessker, si yal lois, anagi, imiren ur ippili tesriê i wid ijehlen, u nitni ur ste$fiôen

# 1986

Mi walan, imednas, aâaqeb, ur ippifsus fellasen, ur ppestaâfun.

# 1987

Mi walan, wid ipcaraken, wid curken, ad inin: "a Mass nne$! D wigi i d icriken nne$ u$uô nepnuju, war Keçç". Ad asen d rren: "kunwi, war ccekk, d ikeddaben".

# 1988

Assen, ad fken mayna i Öebbi. Itelf iten wayen d snulfuyen.

# 1989

Wid ijehlen, u sîixxiôen seg ubrid n Öebbi, Nerna yasen aâaqeb sennig wayev, ilmend n wayen ssefsaden.

# 1990

Ass ideg ara d Nessker, i yal lois, anagi segsen, fellasen, a k id Nawi d anagi mgal wigi. Nessers ak d Tazmamt, d abeggen n yal cci, d nnhaya, d aêunu, u d abecceô i imvuâen.

# 1991

Ih, Öebbi Iumeô ed lêeqq, akked lewqama, talalt i llzem. Igdel tucmitin, ayen n dir, ddeôk. A kwen Ipnabi, amar a d temmektim.

# 1992

Eîîfet di lemâahda n Öebbi ma tâahdem. Ur êentet di tgallit ma tetebbtem, u tcubkem Öebbi. Ih, Öebbi Iéôa acu txeddmem.

# 1993

Ur cebbut tin ifsin lxiv is, mbaâd ma tcudd it, s loehd. Tepparam tagallit nnwen i umkellex garawen: ad ikk lois sennig wayev. Öebbi Ipjeôôib ikwen kan, yis. War ccekk, ad awen Ibeggen, ass n tnekra, ayen i$ef temgarradem.

# 1994

Lemmer i S ihwi, i Öebbi, a kwen Irr d yiwen n lois. Maca, Itellif win i S ihwan, Inehhu win i S ihwan. S tidep, a ppepusteqsim $ef wayen txeddmem.

# 1995

Ur pparat tagallit nnwen i umkellex garawen. Ad iccev uvaô mbaâd ma iîîef. A pjeôbem tawa$it, ilmend n wayen tveôôfem seg ubrid n Öebbi. I kunwi, aâaqeb abarar.

# 1996

Ur ppa$et s lemâahda n Öebbi ayen ôxisen. Ih, yif it i kunwi wayen illan $eô Öebbi, lemmer teéôim.

# 1997

Ayen illan $uôwen, ad ifukk; ayen illan $eô Öebbi, ad idum. War ccekk, a Nkafi wid iûebôen, s wazal n wayen xeddmen ifuqen.

# 1998

Wid ixeddmen ayen ilhan, d ddkeô ne$ d nnta, u umnen, a ten Nessider di tmeddurt tumâint, a ten Nkafi s wazal n wayen xeddmen ifuqen.

# 1999

Mara te$ôev Leqwôan, ssuter a k Iaâteq Öebbi, si Cciîan imenfi.

# 2000

Neppa, s tidep, ur isâi adabu $ef wid iumnen, i ippeklen $ef Mass nnsen.

# 2001

Adabu ines, $ef wid kan i t irran d bab, d wid i S ipcaraken.

# 2002

Ma Nbeddel assekni s ussekni, u Öebbi Yif akw akken Issen ayen id Issers, a d inin: "keçç, d win kan id isnulfuyen". Xaîi! Tegwti, degsen, ur ssinen.

# 2003

Ini: "Issers it id ôôuê iôqan, s$uô Mass ik, s tidep, iwakken ad itebbet wid iumnen; d nnhaya u d abecceô i imvuâen".

# 2004

Ih, Neéôa, qqaôen: "d amdan kan it isselmaden". Tameslayt n win d gren, d tabeôôanit, wagi d awal aâôab n ûûeê.

# 2005

Ih, wid ur numin ara s issekniyen n Öebbi, ur ten Inehhu Öebbi. I nitni, aâaqeb aqeôêan.

# 2006

Ih, gren d kan tikerkas, wid ur numin ara s issekniyen n Öebbi. Widak, d nitni ay d ikeddaben.

# 2007

Win inekôen Öebbi, deffir liman is, siwa ma êeppmen fellas, u ul is izga iumen.... Ma d wid illin idmaren nnsen, ar tijehli, ad Izâaf Öebbi fellasen. Fellasen aâaqeb abarar.

# 2008

Ayagi, acku smenyafen tameddurt n ddunit i laxeôt. Ih, Öebbi ur Inehhu agdud ijehliyen.

# 2009

D wigi iwumi Isle$ Öebbi ulawen nnsen, timejjin nnsen, iéôi nnsen. Wigi d i$efliyen.

# 2010

War ccekk, nitni, di laxeôt, ad ilin d imexsuôen.

# 2011

Sinna, Mass ik, s tidep, i wid iunagen mbaâd ma thewwlen, sinna juhden, ûebôen; ih, Mass ik, deffir waya, Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu.

# 2012

Ass ideg ara d ias, yal yiwen, ad inamer $ef yiman is, u yal yiwen ad iîîukafi $ef wayen ixdem, nitni ur pwadensen.

# 2013

Ifka d Öebbi amedya n temdint, i illan di laman u îîmana. Ippas ip id ôôeéq is, s lufa, si yal tama. Tenkeô l$it n Öebbi. Isukk Öebbi fellas tawa$it n llaé akked lweêc, ilmend n wayen la ûûenâan.

# 2014

Ni$ iusa ten id umazan, segsen. Skaddben t, iwwet iten uâaqeb, nitni densen.

# 2015

Eççet seg wayen is ikwen I$at Öebbi, i iêellen, i imaânen. Snemmret l$it n Öebbi, ma d Neppa ay tâabdem.

# 2016

I yawen Igdel siwa loifa, idim, aksum n yilef, akked wayen id irsen s yisem ur nelli d win n Öebbi. Ma d win terra tmara, ur ijuô, ur inufeq, Öebbi, s tidep, Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu.

# 2017

Ur qqaôet tikerkas id ppawin ilsawen nnwen: "aya d leêlal, aya d leêôam". A d tegrem tikerkas $ef Öebbi. Wid id iggaren tikerkas $ef Öebbi, ur rebêen.

# 2018

Drus ara zhun, fellasen aâaqeb aqeôêan.

# 2019

I wudayen, Negdel ayen i$ef i k Neêka, iu$ lêal. Ur ten Nednis, maca nitni ddennisen iman nnsen.

# 2020

Sinna, Mass ik, i wid ixedmen cceôô, ur ssinen, d$a steôoâen deffir waya, u sweqmen, Mass ik, war ccekk, deffir waya, Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu.

# 2021

Ibôahim, ih, d amdan i imalen ar tidep, i iunzen i Öebbi. Ur illi seg imcurak.

# 2022

Isnemmar l$it iS. Ifren it u Inha t s abrid uwqim.

# 2023

Nefka yas di ddunit ise$, u, di laxeôt, neppa, s tidep, ad yili seg izedganen.

# 2024

Sinna, Nweêêa yak d a ppedduv d ddin n Ibôahim, i imalen ar tidep. Ur illi seg imcurak.

# 2025

Ssebt, iu$al kan i wid imgarraden fellas. Ih, Mass ik ad Iêudd garasen, ass n tnekra, $ef wayen llan mgarraden.

# 2026

Enced s abrid n Mass ik, s ûûwab akked nnhaya tumâint. Mmeslay iten, s yiles aéidan mavi. Ih, Mass ik Yif akw akken Issen, anwi i iff$en seg ubrid iS. Neppa Yif akw akken Issen, anwi i ipwanhan.

# 2027

Ma tâaqbem, âaqbet akken teppuâaqbem. Ma tûebôem, yif it i iûebôiyen.

# 2028

Eûbeô. Üûebô ik s Öebbi kan. Ur $webben ilmend nnsen, ur pveyyiq si tcengal nnsen.

# 2029

Ih, Öebbi Atan ar wid ipêezziben, akked wid issewqamen.

# 2030

Gedha s Win Ibbwin amdan iS, d iminig n yiv, si Loamaâ n Lêaôam, ar Loamaâ ibaâden mavi, ideg Neôqa i as d izzin, iwakken ad as Nessken, seg issekniyen nne£. Ih, Neppa, d Win Isellen, Ipwalin.

# 2031

Nefka Tazmamt i Musa, u Nerra p d nnhaya i At Isôail. "Ur sâut awkil, war Nek".

# 2032

D tarwa n wid i Nebbwi akked Nuê. Neppa, s tidep, d amdan isnemmiren.

# 2033

Nsseyya di Tezmamt, i At Isôail: "war ccekk, a ppesfesdem, di tmurt, berdayen, u aîas ara tesme$wôem iman nnwen".

# 2034

Mi d iusa usefsed amenzu segsen, Nuzen awen d imdanen nne£, s loehd uqsiê, kecmen ixxamen; lemâahda tevôa.

# 2035

Sinna, Nerra d ppaô nnwen, segsen. Nebbwi yawen d ayla, tarwa. Nesîuqqet iâsekôiwen nnwen.

# 2036

Ma tmaânem, i iman nnwen, ma tdensem, i iman nnwen. Mi d tusa lemâahda taneggarut, ssexven udmawen nnwen, kecmen Loamaâ, akken i t kecmen abrid amenzu; hudden, wakali, ayen is ipzuxxun.

# 2037

Ahat Mass nnwen ad Iêun fellawen. Ma tulsem, a Nales. Nerra Loahennama d lêebs i ijehliyen.

# 2038

Ih, Leqwôan agi inehhu ar wayen iweqmen mavi, ibecceô lmumnin i ixeddmen ayen ilhan, ar i nitni akafi meqqwôen.

# 2039

Wanag wid ur numin ara s laxeôt, Nhegga yasen d aâaqeb aqeôêan.

# 2040

Amdan issawal i cceôô, akken issawal i lxiô. Amdan izga d aêemmaq.

# 2041

Nerra, iv akked wass, d sin issekniyen. Assekni n yiv Nerra d tellis, Nerra win n wass d win ipwalin, iwakken a pnadim lfevl n Mass nnwen, a ppissinem amvan iseggwasen, akked leêsab. Yal ta$awsa, Nfeûûel ip akken iwata.

# 2042

I yal amdan, Ncudd as lbext is s amgarv is. Ass n tnekra, ad as d Nessuffe$ tazmamt ara iaf teldi.

# 2043

"£eô tazmamt ik! Tqaddev, assa, s yiman ik, i uqeîîi k".

# 2044

Win ipwanhan, i iman is kan, win innetlafen, innetlaf mgal iman is kan. Ur ipbibbi yiwen taâkkwemt n wayev. Ur Nekkat, alamma Nuzen amazan.

# 2045

Ma Neb$a a Nesqucc tamdint, Neppak lameô i isâiyen is, ad xedmen, degs, cceôô. Ad iâaddi fellas Wawal, a p Nhudd wakali.

# 2046

Acêal n tsuta ay Nesqucc, deffir Nuê! Ad Iqadd Mass ik, i tussna akked tmeéôiwt ibekkaven n imdanen iS.

# 2047

Win ib$an taêemmaqt, Nezzazzal as degs, i £ ihwan, i win i £ Neb$a. Sinna, Nerra yas Loahennama ad din iô$, indell, ippuveggeô.

# 2048

Win ib$an laxeôt, iaâzem fellas yal laâzem, u neppa iumen; widak, tajmilt i laâzem nnsen.

# 2049

I akw, i wigi d wiyav, Nwessaâ tikci s$uô Mass ik. Tikci n Mass ik, ur meêdudet.

# 2050

Wali amek Nesmenyaf kra i wiyav. War ccekk, di laxeôt, lfeôq d usmenyef, ad ilin sennig waya.

# 2051

Ur sâu, ar tama n Öebbi, ôebbi nniven, mulac a ppu$alev d imdelli, d imveggaâ.

# 2052

Iseyya d Mass ik: ur tâabdem siwa Neppa, elhut ar imawlan. Ma, $uôek wesser yiwen, ne$ ma wessren i sin, ur asen qqaô: "ttfuh"! Ur ten ppara. Mmeslay asen s lkyasa.

# 2053

Zger fellasen tacvat n lmaênana. Ini: "a Mass iw! Ëun fellasen, akken iyi d ssekren d amejtuê".

# 2054

Mass nnwen Yif akw akken Issen, i illan deg iman nnwen. Ma telham, Neppa, s tidep, Ipsemmiê wid isteôoiâen.

# 2055

Efk i llezm ik amur is, akw i ume$bun akked win d ibbwi ubrid. Ur pjeggiê d ajeggeê.

# 2056

Ijeggaêen, s tidep, d atmaten n Cciîan. Cciîan ijhel ar Mass is.

# 2057

# 2846

Qaôun, Ferâun, Haman, ni$ iusa ten id Musa, s ubeggen. Sme$wôen iman nnsen, di tmurt, ur rbiêen.

# 3380

Yal wa, Newwet it $ef ubekkav is. Llan wid iwumi Nuzen tabucivant. Llan wid i iwwet usu$u. Llan wid i Nger seddaw wakal. Llan wid i Ne$meq. Maççi d Öebbi iten idensen, d nitni i idensen iman nnsen.

# 3381

# 3382

# 3383

# 3384

# 3385

# 3386

Ur pnamaret At Tezmamt, siwa s wawal aéidan, siwa wid degsen idensen. Init: "numen s wayen id irsen $uône$, id irsen $uôwen. Öebbi nne$, akked Öebbi nnwen, Yiwen. Nekwni $uôeS d imvuâen".

# 3387

# 3388

# 3391

# 3400

# 3401

# 3402

# 3403

# 3429

# 3430

# 3431

# 3433

# 3498

# 3501

# 5076

# 5079

# 5080

# 5082

# 5083

# 5084

# 5085

Acu ikwen iu$en, ur tepseddiqem deg ubrid n Öebbi? N Öebbi lweôt n tmurt akked igenwan. Ur taâdilem ara: wid iseddqen uqbel l$elb, u nnu$en, widak, ad aâlayen, nezzeh, sennig wid iseddqen sin $er da, u nnu$en. Iwaââed asen akw Öebbi ûûam. Öebbi Iéôa ayen txedmem.

# 5086

Win iôevlen i Öebbi aôeîîal umâin, ad as d Irr s lufa, u ines warraz ukyis.

# 5087

Asmi ara twaliv lmumnin, argaz tameîîut, teddun tafat nnsen zdat sen, u yeffus nnsen: "a lxiô nnwen, assa, di leonanat, ddawat sen isaffen ppazzalen, degsen a pwekkôem! D wagi ay d rrbeê ameqwôaêan".

# 5088

Ass ideg ixabiten, argaz tameîîut, ad inin i wid iumnen: "arout a$, a neddem si tafat nnwen"! A d inin: "u$alet ar deffir, a d tqelbem tafat"! Ad yili garasen lêiv, s tebburt. Zdaxel d aêunu, beôôa, zdat es: aâaqeb.

# 5089

Ad sen d siwlen: "day ur nella ara yidwen"? Ad inin: "ih! Maca, thewwlem iman nnwen, tekkukram, tcukkem, $elvent kwen lemcihwat, armi d iusa lameô n Öebbi. I$elv ikwen af Öebbi, u$ellav".

# 5090

Assa, ur ipwaîîaf feddu segwen, ne$ seg wid ijehlen. Axxam nnwen d times; d neppat ay d bab nnwen. A tu$alin tucmip!

# 5091

# 5092

Ecfut ar Öebbi Issidir tamurt, deffir tmeppant is. Ni$ Nbeggen awen d issekniyen, amendeô ma a pfehmem?

# 5093

# 5094

Wid iumnen s Öebbi akked imazanen iS, d nitni ay d iêeqqiyen, u d inagan ar Mass nnsen. Ad awin arraz nnsen akked tafat nnsen. Wid ijehlen u skaddben issekniyen nne£, widak d at ujajiê.

# 5095

Cfut ar tameddurt n ddunit d urar kan, d zzhu, d acebbeê, d zzux garawen, asuget n wayla akked derya. Am umedya ugeffur. Im$an is âaoben ijehliyen; sinna, ad isliwen, a ten twaliv ppiwôi$en; d$a ad êevmen. Di laxeôt, aâaqeb uqsiê akked ssmaê s$uô Öebbi, akked llza. Tameddurt n ddunit d zzehwa kan ip$uôôun.

# 5096

£iwlet ar ssmaê n Mass nnwen, akked Loennet iwesâan am tmurt akked igenni, teppuhegga d i wid iumnen s Öebbi akked imazanen iS. D wagi ay d lfevl n Öebbi. Ippak it i win i S ihwan. Öebbi d Bab n lfevl ameqwôaêan.

# 5097

Ur d tveôôu twa$it di tmurt, ne$ deg iman nnwen, siwa ma tura di Tezmamt, uqbel a p id Nawi. Ayagi, s tidep, d ayen isehlen i Öebbi.

# 5098

# 5100

Nuzen ed imazanen nne£, s ubeggen. Nessader ed yidsen Tazmamt akked lmizan, iwakken ad ddun imdanen s lêeqq. Nessader ed uzzal, degs vveôô uqsiê, akked uba$uô i medden, iwakken ad Iéeô Öebbi anwa ara ifken afus i Neppa akked imazanen iS, di tbavnit. Ih, Öebbi d Uohid, d Uzmir.

# 5101

Ni$ Nuzen ed Nuê akked Ibôahim. Nerra, si tarwa nnsen, Lambiyya, Tira. Degsen llan wid ipwanhan; aîas segsen d iballa$en.

# 5102

Sinna, Nessevfeô ed, deffir sen, imazanen nne$. Nessevfeô ed Âisa, mmi s n Meryem, Nefka yas Linoil. Nessekcem deg ulawen n wid iddan yides leênana akked tiéeî. Taxelwit, ur p Nuri fellasen; snulfan p id i llza n Öebbi. Ur qumen ara yis, akken iwata. Nefka arraz nnsen i wid iumnen segsen. Aîas, segsen, d iballa$en.

# 5103

A wid iumnen! Ëezzbet i Öebbi. Amnet s Umazan iS. Ad awen Ifk sin imuren seg uêunu S, ad awen Irr tafat a ppeddum yis, ad awen Isemmeê. Öebbi Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu.

# 5104

# 5105

Ni$ Isla Öebbi i wawal n tin i k d ihedôen $ef urgaz is. Tepcetkay i Öebbi. Öebbi Isla i umeslay nnwen. Öebbi, s tidep, Isell, Iéeô.

# 5106

Wid ipmettilen tilawin nnsen ar izugar n tyimmatin nnsen, ur llint d tiyimmatin nnsen - imi tiyimmatin d tid, kan, i ten id iurwen -, ihi, ar d nnan yir awal, akked tikerkas. Ih, Öebbi ard Win Ipsemmiêen, Ipqilin.

# 5107

Wid imetlen, akka, tilawin nnsen, sinna, wexxôen i wayen d nnan, ad brun i wakli, uqbel a tent nnalen. D ayen u$uô i kwen nuban. Öebbi Iéôa ayen txedmem.

# 5108

Win ur newâa ara, ilaq ad iuéum sin wagguren, wa deffir wa, uqbel a p innal. Win, da$en, ur nezmir ara, ad icceçç sdiset igellilen. Akka, iwakken a ppamnem s Öebbi akked Umazan iS. D tigi ay d tilisa n Öebbi. I ijehliyen aâaqeb aqeôêan.

# 5109

Ih, wid ipqamaôen Öebbi akked Umazan iS, ad nneqlaben, akken nneqlaben wid i ten id izwaren. Ni$ Nessers ed issekniyen iberrzen. I ijehliyen, aâaqeb isdullun.

# 5110

Ass ideg ara ten id Issker Öebbi, meôôa, ad asen Issken ayen xedmen. Öebbi Iêesb iten, nitni ppun ten. Öebbi d Anagi n yal cci.

# 5111

Day ur twalav ara ar Öebbi Iéôa i illan di tmurt, i illan deg igenwan? Ur ippili wawal ger krav, mebla ma Illa, Neppa, d wis kué; ne$ ger smus, u Neppa, d wis sdis. Ama seddaw, ne$ sennig waya, ad Yili yidsen, anda ma llan. D$a, ad asen Imel acu xedmen, ass n tnekra. Ih, Öebbi Iéôa yal cci.

# 5112

Ur twalav ara wid i$ef tepwagdel temlilit i umeslay, sinna, u$alen ar wayen i sen ipwagedlen? Ppemlilin i ubekkav, i wanfal, i âaûûu i Umazan. Ma usan k id, ad sellmen fellak s wayen ur d Ipsellim fellak Öebbi. Qqaôen deg ulawen nnsen: "awi d kan ur a$ Ipâuqub ara Öebbi $ef wayen neqqaô"! Loahennama beôka ten. Ad ô$en degs. A tu$alin icemten!

# 5113

A wid iumnen! Ma temlalem i wawal, ur ppemlilit ara i ubekkav, i wanfal, i âaûûu i Umazan. Ppemlilit i tezdeg akked uêezzeb. Ëezzbet i Öebbi u$uô ara tepwafesrem.

# 5114

Timlilit i wawal si Cciîan kan, iwakken ad $weblen wid iumnen. Acemma ur ten iîîuôôu, siwa ma Irad Öebbi. £ef Öebbi ara ppeklen lmumnin.

# 5115

A wid iumnen! Ma nnan awen: "get amkan" di temliliyin, get amkan! Öebbi ad awen Ig amkan. Ma nnan awen: "ooet amkan", ooet amkan! Ad Issali Öebbi tidekkaôin, wid iumnen segwen, akked wid iwumi teppunefk tmusni. Öebbi Iéôa ayen txedmem.

# 5116

A wid iumnen! Ma temlalem i wawal akked Umazan, seddqet uqbel timlilit. Akka i wen ilha, i wen iûfa. Ma ur tewâam ara, ihi, Öebbi Ipsemmiê, Ipêunu.

# 5117

Tekukram a pseddqem uqbel timlilit nnwen? Ma ur tseddqem ara, u Issuref awen Öebbi, ééallet, zekkit, a$et awal i Öebbi akked Umazan iS. Öebbi Iéôa ayen txedmem.

# 5118

Day ur twalav ara wid idduklen akked ugdud i$ef Izzaâf Öebbi? Ur llin segwen ne$ segsen. Pgalan s tkerkas, u nitni éôan.

# 5119

# 5120

£ilen tagallit nnsen d ssôan. Swexxiôen seg ubrid n Öebbi. Fellasen aâaqeb isdullun.

# 5121

Ur sen d ippawi acemma wayla nnsen, ne$ dderya nnsen, mgal Öebbi, d awez$i. Widak d at tmes. Degs, nitni, ad wekkôen.

# 5122

Ass ideg ara ten id Issker Öebbi, meôôa, ad aS gallen akken i wen pgallan. Ad $ilen ar ad yili wacu ideg ara îîfen. Aâni maççi, war ccekk, nitni d ikeddaben?

# 5123

Imelk iten Cciîan armi ppun asmekti n Öebbi. Widak d akabar n Cciîan. Ni$ akabar n Cciîan d imexsuôen.

# 5124

Ih, wid ipqamaôen Öebbi akked Umazan iS, widak, ad ndellen sennig wiyav.

# 5125

Iura Öebbi: war ccekk, d Nek akked imazanen iW, ara irebêen. Öebbi, s tidep, d Uohid, d Uzmir.

# 5126

Ur teppafev ara agdud iumnen s Öebbi akked wass aneggaru, ad iddukwel akked wid ipqamaôen Öebbi akked Umazan iS. Xas ma llan d ibabaten nnsen, ne$ d arraw nnsen, d atmaten nnsen, d alag nnsen. Widak, Iura yasen liman deg ulawen nnsen, Iul iten s ôôuê s$uôeS. A ten Issekcem di leonanat, ddawat sen isaffen ppazzalen, degsen ad wekkôen. Öuvan Öebbi, Iôuva ten. Widak d akabar n Öebbi. Day akabar n Öebbi maççi d win ara irebêen?

# 5127

Sbuccuâen Öebbi kra illan deg igenwan, akked kra illan di tmurt. Neppa d Uzmir, d Bab n ûûwab.

# 5128

D Neppa i Issuff$en seg ixxamen nnsen wid ijehlen seg At Tezmamt, i ujemmal amezwaru. Ur tuminem ara ad ff$en. £ilen leswaô nnsen a ten sellken si Öebbi. Ikka yasen d Öebbi seg wanda ur bnin. Issekcem tugdi deg ulawen nnsen. Hudden ixxamen nnsen, s ifassen nnsen, akked ifassen n lmumnin. Meyyzet a wid ipwalin!

# 5129

Lemmer ur asen Iura ara Öebbi neffu, yili Iqeîîa ten di ddunit, u, di laxeôt, fellasen aâaqeb n tmes.

# 5130

Ayagi, acku numren Öebbi akked Umazan iS. Win inumren Öebbi, ihi, Öebbi, Iwâaô i uqeîîi.

# 5131

Ayen tgezmem n tezdayin akked wayen teooam beddent af iéuôan nnsent, s wannuf n Öebbi, iwakken a d Isdull iballa$en.

# 5132

Ayen i s Ifka Öebbi, s$uôsen, i Umazan iS, ur tebgisem fellas s ioedâen akked lemrakeb. Maca, Öebbi Ippak adabu i Umazan iS, $ef wid i S ihwan. Öebbi Izmer i yal cci.

# 5133

Ayen Ifka Öebbi i Umazan iS, s$uô at tuddar, n Öebbi akked Umazan iS, llezm is, igujilen, ime$ban, akked win d ibbwi ubrid. Iwakken ur ippu$al ara ger ifassen imeôkantiyen nnwen. Ayen i wen ifka Umazan, ddmet ep. Ayen i wen ikkes, kkset ep. Ëezzbet i Öebbi. Ih, Öebbi, Iwâaô i uqeîîi.

# 5134

I igellilen iminigen, id ssuff$en seg ixxamen nnsen akked seg wayla nnsen, ssaramen lfevl n Öebbi akked llza, fkan afus i Öebbi akked Umazan iS, d widak ay d imawlan n tidep.

# 5135

Wid ized$en ixxamen, iumnen uqbel nnsen, êemmlen wid id iunagen $uôsen. Ur néifen idmaren nnsen af wayen i sen ippunefken, smenyafen ten i iman nnsen, xas ma gwran d xuûûen. Wid irran akin ccêa af yiman nnsen, widak d imerbaê.

# 5136

Wid id iusan deffir sen, qqaôen: "a Mass nne$! Semmeê a$, akked wamaten nne$, i $ d izwaren ar liman. Ur Ppara deg ulawen nne$, a$ullu n wid iumnen. A Mass nne$! Keçç, s tidep, d Umâin Ipêunun".

# 5137

Ur twalav ara ixabiten, la qqaôen i watmaten nnsen ijehlen, seg wAt Tezmamt: "ma ssuff$en kwen, ard a neffe$ yidwen, ur nessemêas i yiwen, d awez$i, mgal nnwen. Ma nnu$en kwen, ar ad awen nefk afus". Ad Icehhed Öebbi, ar nitni d ikeddaben.

# 5138

Ma ssuff$en ten, ur teff$en yidsen. Ma nnu$en ten, ur asen ppaken afus. Ma âawnen ten, ad rewlen; ihi, ur ppâawanen!

# 5139

D kunwi, sennig Öebbi, ay ugaden idmaren nnsen, ayagi, acku nitni d agdud ur nefhim.

# 5140

Ur kwen pna$en, ddukwlen, siwa ma di temdinin ippwaéeôben, ne$ deffir leswaô. Lbe$wv garasen qesseê. A pxilev dduklen, wanag rwin wulawen nnsen. Ayagi, acku nitni d agdud ur nepxemmim.

# 5141

Cban wid i ten id izwaren s cwiî kan, jeôôben lwexda igiten nnsen, fellasen aâaqeb aqeôêan.

# 5142
